## User

pelajari isi html waltrust . https://luma.com/4x4xj87m?tk=jC6eMp  aku semalam lupa ikut ini dan pengen ikut https://tatum.io/tatum-x-walrus-hackathon .  tapi belum ada ide yang keren dan juara 1 agar menang. Jika kamu seorang profesional top dunia web3 sebagai BD,Comunnity anager, Marketing Manager, dan Dev web3 di SUI, buatkan ide 5 terbaik agar project menang  juara 1 serta project benar-benar dibutuhkan ekosistem SUI , tatum, dan web3. Oke, gue udah baca semua detail hackathon-nya. Ini serius, deadline 6 Juni 2026 ŌĆö masih ada waktu sekitar 11 hari. Prize pool $2K dari Tatum x Walrus, judging 30% Walrus+Tatum integration, 30% technical quality, 20% creativity, 20% presentation.
Sekarang sebagai BD + Community Manager + Marketing Manager + Web3 Dev SUI ŌĆö ini 5 ide terbaik yang punya peluang juara 1: Oke bro, ini breakdown strategis dari perspektif BD + DevRel + Marketing + Dev:

Kenapa WalTrust (Ide #1) paling berpeluang juara 1:
Ini menyentuh 3 pain point sekaligus ŌĆö ekosistem SUI butuh killer app di luar DeFi, Walrus butuh use case nyata yang bukan sekadar "IPFS tapi lebih baik", dan Tatum butuh showcase bahwa RPC mereka dipakai di app production-grade. Credential verification adalah masalah universal yang semua orang mengerti, jadi demo video-nya mudah dijelaskan dalam 2 menit.
Dari sisi judging, Walrus dipakai untuk core function (simpan dokumen PDF/gambar ijazah), bukan sekedar add-on. Itu penting banget karena requirement mereka bilang "integrate Walrus meaningfully, not just as an add-on."
Tips marketing untuk bonus poin:
Langsung post di X tagging @Tatum_io, @WalrusFoundation, dan @SuiNetwork begitu launch. Ini eksplisit disebutkan di rules sebagai bonus poin. Sekarang gue akan buat dokumen blueprint WalTrust yang sangat detail dan mendalam ŌĆö dari perspektif juri top dunia Web3 Tatum + Walrus. Ini bukan sekadar overview, tapi full technical specification + judging strategy. build sekarang secara komprehensif.

# Walrus Workshop: Sui Overflow

Hosted by Amogh, Abner & Walrus Foundation

Zoom

Registration

Past Event

Welcome! To join the event, please register below.

Register

You will be asked to verify token ownership with your wallet.

About Event

ŌĆŗA 90-minute hands-on workshop where you'll ship a working app with Walrus Memory, the user-owned memory layer on Walrus. Memory that persists across sessions, models, and devices, with on-chain authorization for sharing and revocation.

ŌĆŗ**$70K up for grabs:** The Walrus track at Sui Overflow 2026 has a $70,000 USD prize pool. This workshop is designed to get you from zero to a submission-ready foundation in 90 minutes.

ŌĆŗ**What you'll build:** A minimal Next.js app (think reading tracker or decisions log) wired up with Walrus Memory end-to-end. By the end of the session, you'll have a deployable starting point you can extend for your Overflow submission.

ŌĆŗ**What you'll learn**

-   ŌĆŗReading and writing to Walrus Memory from a Next.js app
    
-   ŌĆŗHow on-chain key authorization works for granting app and collaborator access
    
-   ŌĆŗRevoking access in a single on-chain action
    
-   ŌĆŗThe current shape of sharing today, and where scoped and read-only sharing is headed
    

ŌĆŗ**Who this is for:** Overflow builders who want user-owned memory primitives in their stack and plan to compete in the Walrus track, or anyone curious about what Walrus enables beyond raw storage.

ŌĆŗ**When:** Monday, May 25, 2026 ┬Ę 2:00 pm UTC  
**Duration:** 90 minutes

Tatum x Build on Sui with Walrus

Store. Build. Ship. Use Walrus decentralized storage on Sui, powered by Tatum.

Free to join Remote ┬Ę Global $2,000 USD in prizes May 23 to June 6

[Get Sui API Key](https://dashboard.tatum.io/) [Join Tatum Discord](https://discord.gg/Ttp9zJwPqa) [Submit Project](https://docs.google.com/forms/d/e/1FAIpQLSdPaKcfTbS49ngThDE9Xap7_xkLFrQOISCPHGKJ3FL1drchTw/viewform?usp=publish-editor)

­¤Åå $2,000 USD Prize Pool Sponsored by Tatum x Walrus

### Kickoff May 23rd to Submit by June 6th

Use Tatum's enterprise-grade Sui RPCs and **Walrus decentralized storage** to build apps that actually ship to mainnet. Store data on-chain with Walrus, connect via Tatum's Sui nodes, and build anything: games, DeFi, social tools, or infra. The best Walrus integrations win.

**Kickoff**May 23rd

**Build**May 23 to Jun 6

**Deadline**June 6th, 17:00 UTC

**Results**June 7th

#### ­¤ÜĆ Fun Project Ideas using Walrus

Decentralized Storage Apps On-chain Media DeFi + Data AI + Walrus Gaming Assets Social Protocols Infra and Tooling

Walrus lets you store blobs of data on Sui in a decentralized way. Think NFT metadata, game state, social content, or any app that needs trustless storage.

#### ­¤øĀ’ĖÅ Requirements

-   Use a **Tatum API key** (free via [dashboard.tatum.io](https://dashboard.tatum.io/)) and Tatum's Sui RPC nodes
-   **Integrate Walrus** storage meaningfully in your project
-   Build on **Sui Mainnet** (preferred) or Testnet/Devnet
-   **MCP optional** but encouraged for AI features ([docs](https://tatum.io/mcp))
-   Team size: **1 to 3 members**
-   Submit a GitHub repo + **2 to 3 min demo video** via the [submission form](https://docs.google.com/forms/d/e/1FAIpQLSdPaKcfTbS49ngThDE9Xap7_xkLFrQOISCPHGKJ3FL1drchTw/viewform?usp=publish-editor)

#### ­¤Åå Prizes - $2,000 USD Total

**­¤źć 1st**$600 USD

#### ŌÜ¢’ĖÅ Judging Criteria

-   **Walrus and Tatum Integration (30%)** - Meaningful, creative use of Walrus Data and storage on Sui as well as building with Tatum RPCs or Data APIs

-   **Creativity (20%)**
-   **Presentation (20%)** - Clear docs and a working demo

Ō¢Č ­¤ÆŠ What is Walrus?

Walrus is a decentralized storage and data availability protocol built on Sui. It allows you to store large blobs of data such as images, files, game state, and metadata in a trustless, cost-efficient way, directly accessible from your Sui smart contracts and dApps.

For this hackathon, **your project must use Walrus** as part of its core functionality, not just as an add-on.

[Walrus Website](https://walrus.xyz) ┬Ę [Walrus Docs](https://docs.wal.app) ┬Ę [Walrus Discord](https://discord.com/invite/walrusprotocol)

570: 
571: <!-- ==================== SECTION 1: OVERVIEW ==================== -->
572: <section class="section" id="overview">
573:   <div class="container">
574:     <div class="section-label" data-num="01">PROJECT OVERVIEW</div>
575:     <h2 class="section-title">Apa itu WalTrust?</h2>
576:     <p class="section-desc">Platform verifikasi kredensial Web3 pertama di ekosistem SUI. Institusi menerbitkan credential, user menyimpannya di Walrus, employer memverifikasi on-chain dalam hitungan detik.</p>
577: 
578:     <div class="callout callout-green">
579:       <span class="callout-icon">­¤Ä»</span>
580:       <div class="callout-text">
581:         <strong>Positioning sebagai Juri:</strong> "WalTrust adalah satu-satunya proyek yang membuktikan bahwa Walrus bukan sekadar 'IPFS yang lebih murah' ŌĆö tapi infrastructure untuk trust layer baru di internet. Ini adalah killer app yang ekosistem SUI butuhkan."
582:       </div>
583:     </div>
584: 
585:     <div class="grid-2" style="gap:1rem; margin-top:1.5rem;">
586:       <div class="card card-green">
587:         <h4>Problem Statement</h4>
588:         <p>Credential verification hari ini: lambat (hariŌĆōminggu), mahal (biaya administrasi), mudah dipalsukan, dan terpusat di satu institusi. LinkedIn bisa diisi sembarangan, ijazah bisa dipalsukan, sertifikasi expired tidak ter-update.</p>
589:       </div>
590:       <div class="card card-blue">
591:         <h4>Solution</h4>
592:         <p>Institusi (univ, lembaga sertifikasi) menerbitkan credential sebagai signed attestation di SUI. Dokumen asli disimpan di Walrus. Employer query langsung ke SUI + Walrus via Tatum RPC. Verification: &lt; 3 detik. Biaya: &lt; $0.01.</p>
593:       </div>
594:     </div>
595: 
596:     <h3>User Roles & Flow</h3>
597:     <div class="grid-3" style="margin-top: 0.5rem;">
598:       <div class="card">
599:         <div class="arch-label" style="text-align:left; color: var(--green);">ROLE 1</div>
600:         <div class="arch-name" style="text-align:left; font-size:15px; font-weight:600; margin-bottom:6px;">Issuer</div>
601:         <ul class="checklist">
602:           <li><span class="check-icon">Ō£ō</span> Universitas / lembaga sertifikasi</li>
603:           <li><span class="check-icon">Ō£ō</span> Upload dokumen ke Walrus</li>
604:           <li><span class="check-icon">Ō£ō</span> Sign & issue credential di SUI</li>
605:           <li><span class="check-icon">Ō£ō</span> Revoke jika perlu</li>
606:         </ul>
607:       </div>
608:       <div class="card">
609:         <div class="arch-label" style="text-align:left; color: var(--blue);">ROLE 2</div>
610:         <div class="arch-name" style="text-align:left; font-size:15px; font-weight:600; margin-bottom:6px;">Holder</div>
611:         <ul class="checklist">
612:           <li><span class="check-icon">Ō£ō</span> Job seeker / profesional</li>
613:           <li><span class="check-icon">Ō£ō</span> Manage wallet credentials</li>
614:           <li><span class="check-icon">Ō£ō</span> Share credential link ke employer</li>
615:           <li><span class="check-icon">Ō£ō</span> Control akses dokumen</li>
616:         </ul>
617:       </div>
618:       <div class="card">
619:         <div class="arch-label" style="text-align:left; color: var(--amber);">ROLE 3</div>
620:         <div class="arch-name" style="text-align:left; font-size:15px; font-weight:600; margin-bottom:6px;">Verifier</div>
621:         <ul class="checklist">
622:           <li><span class="check-icon">Ō£ō</span> Employer / HR / recruiter</li>
623:           <li><span class="check-icon">Ō£ō</span> Paste wallet address / credential ID</li>
624:           <li><span class="check-icon">Ō£ō</span> Instant on-chain verification</li>
625:           <li><span class="check-icon">Ō£ō</span> Lihat dokumen dari Walrus</li>
626:         </ul>
627:       </div>
628:     </div>
629:   </div>
630: </section>
631:

644: 
645:     <h3>Cara memenangkan tiap kategori</h3>
646:     <div class="table-wrap">
647:       <table>
648:         <thead>
649:           <tr>
650:             <th>Kategori</th>
651:             <th>Yang Juri Lihat</th>
652:             <th>Implementasi WalTrust</th>
653:             <th>Bobot</th>
654:           </tr>
655:         </thead>
656:         <tbody>
657:           <tr>
658:             <td><strong>Walrus Integration</strong></td>
659:             <td>Walrus dipakai sebagai <em>core</em>, bukan add-on. Meaningful storage.</td>
660:             <td>Semua dokumen credential (PDF/image) + metadata disimpan di Walrus. Blob ID on-chain. Revocation check via Walrus fetch.</td>
661:             <td><span class="tag tag-g">20%</span></td>
662:           </tr>
663:           <tr>
664:             <td><strong>Tatum RPC Usage</strong></td>
665:             <td>Semua on-chain call via Tatum endpoint, bukan public RPC lain.</td>
666:             <td>Semua SuiClient dikonfigurasi ke <code>sui-mainnet.gateway.tatum.io</code> dengan API key. Query credential, event, object via Tatum.</td>
667:             <td><span class="tag tag-g">10%</span></td>
668:           </tr>
669:           <tr>
670:             <td><strong>Technical Quality</strong></td>
671:             <td>Clean Move code, successful deployment mainnet, error handling, README lengkap.</td>
672:             <td>Move module terstruktur, unit test, deploy ke Sui Mainnet, CI/CD, TypeScript SDK, error boundaries di frontend.</td>
673:             <td><span class="tag tag-b">30%</span></td>
674:           </tr>
675:           <tr>
676:             <td><strong>Creativity</strong></td>
677:             <td>Unique use case, solves real problem, tidak generik.</td>
678:             <td>Credential verification adalah masalah nyata milyaran orang. WalTrust = LinkedIn versi trustless. Bukan sekadar "todo app di blockchain".</td>
679:             <td><span class="tag tag-a">20%</span></td>
680:           </tr>
681:           <tr>
682:             <td><strong>Presentation</strong></td>
683:             <td>Demo video 2-3 menit yang jelas, README profesional, live demo link.</td>
684:             <td>Script demo sudah direncanakan. Voiceover storytelling. GitHub README dengan arsitektur diagram + setup guide.</td>
685:             <td><span class="tag tag-a">20%</span></td>
686:           </tr>
687:           <tr>
688:             <td><strong>Bonus: Best Walrus</strong></td>
689:             <td>Most creative + effective Walrus use.</td>
690:             <td>Walrus menyimpan PDF credential + revocation status metadata. Blob ID di-store on-chain. Access revocation in 1 tx.</td>
691:             <td><span class="tag tag-g">+$200</span></td>
692:           </tr>
693:           <tr>
694:             <td><strong>Bonus: Best Tatum</strong></td>
695:             <td>Leverage Tatum RPC, Data API, atau MCP.</td>
696:             <td>Tatum RPC untuk semua query. Tatum Data API untuk transaction history. MCP server untuk AI features (opsional).</td>
697:             <td><span class="tag tag-g">+$200</span></td>
698:           </tr>
699:         </tbody>
700:       </table>
701:     </div>
702: 
703:     <div class="callout callout-amber">
704:       <span class="callout-icon">ŌÜĀ’ĖÅ</span>

571: <!-- ==================== SECTION 1: OVERVIEW ==================== -->
572: <section class="section" id="overview">
573:   <div class="container">
574:     <div class="section-label" data-num="01">PROJECT OVERVIEW</div>
575:     <h2 class="section-title">Apa itu WalTrust?</h2>
576:     <p class="section-desc">Platform verifikasi kredensial Web3 pertama di ekosistem SUI. Institusi menerbitkan credential, user menyimpannya di Walrus, employer memverifikasi on-chain dalam hitungan detik.</p>
577: 
578:     <div class="callout callout-green">
579:       <span class="callout-icon">­¤Ä»</span>
580:       <div class="callout-text">
581:         <strong>Positioning sebagai Juri:</strong> "WalTrust adalah satu-satunya proyek yang membuktikan bahwa Walrus bukan sekadar 'IPFS yang lebih murah' ŌĆö tapi infrastructure untuk trust layer baru di internet. Ini adalah killer app yang ekosistem SUI butuhkan."
582:       </div>
583:     </div>
584: 
585:     <div class="grid-2" style="gap:1rem; margin-top:1.5rem;">
586:       <div class="card card-green">
587:         <h4>Problem Statement</h4>
588:         <p>Credential verification hari ini: lambat (hariŌĆōminggu), mahal (biaya administrasi), mudah dipalsukan, dan terpusat di satu institusi. LinkedIn bisa diisi sembarangan, ijazah bisa dipalsukan, sertifikasi expired tidak ter-update.</p>
589:       </div>
590:       <div class="card card-blue">
591:         <h4>Solution</h4>
592:         <p>Institusi (univ, lembaga sertifikasi) menerbitkan credential sebagai signed attestation di SUI. Dokumen asli disimpan di Walrus. Employer query langsung ke SUI + Walrus via Tatum RPC. Verification: &lt; 3 detik. Biaya: &lt; $0.01.</p>
593:       </div>
594:     </div>
595: 
596:     <h3>User Roles & Flow</h3>
597:     <div class="grid-3" style="margin-top: 0.5rem;">
598:       <div class="card">
599:         <div class="arch-label" style="text-align:left; color: var(--green);">ROLE 1</div>
600:         <div class="arch-name" style="text-align:left; font-size:15px; font-weight:600; margin-bottom:6px;">Issuer</div>
601:         <ul class="checklist">
602:           <li><span class="check-icon">Ō£ō</span> Universitas / lembaga sertifikasi</li>
603:           <li><span class="check-icon">Ō£ō</span> Upload dokumen ke Walrus</li>
604:           <li><span class="check-icon">Ō£ō</span> Sign & issue credential di SUI</li>
605:           <li><span class="check-icon">Ō£ō</span> Revoke jika perlu</li>
606:         </ul>
607:       </div>
608:       <div class="card">
609:         <div class="arch-label" style="text-align:left; color: var(--blue);">ROLE 2</div>
610:         <div class="arch-name" style="text-align:left; font-size:15px; font-weight:600; margin-bottom:6px;">Holder</div>
611:         <ul class="checklist">
612:           <li><span class="check-icon">Ō£ō</span> Job seeker / profesional</li>
613:           <li><span class="check-icon">Ō£ō</span> Manage wallet credentials</li>
614:           <li><span class="check-icon">Ō£ō</span> Share credential link ke employer</li>
615:           <li><span class="check-icon">Ō£ō</span> Control akses dokumen</li>
616:         </ul>
617:       </div>
618:       <div class="card">
619:         <div class="arch-label" style="text-align:left; color: var(--amber);">ROLE 3</div>
620:         <div class="arch-name" style="text-align:left; font-size:15px; font-weight:600; margin-bottom:6px;">Verifier</div>
621:         <ul class="checklist">
622:           <li><span class="check-icon">Ō£ō</span> Employer / HR / recruiter</li>
623:           <li><span class="check-icon">Ō£ō</span> Paste wallet address / credential ID</li>
624:           <li><span class="check-icon">Ō£ō</span> Instant on-chain verification</li>
625:           <li><span class="check-icon">Ō£ō</span> Lihat dokumen dari Walrus</li>
626:         </ul>
627:       </div>
628:     </div>
629:   </div>
630: </section>

644: 
645:     <h3>Cara memenangkan tiap kategori</h3>
646:     <div class="table-wrap">
647:       <table>
648:         <thead>
649:           <tr>
650:             <th>Kategori</th>
651:             <th>Yang Juri Lihat</th>
652:             <th>Implementasi WalTrust</th>
653:             <th>Bobot</th>
654:           </tr>
655:         </thead>
656:         <tbody>
657:           <tr>
658:             <td><strong>Walrus Integration</strong></td>
659:             <td>Walrus dipakai sebagai <em>core</em>, bukan add-on. Meaningful storage.</td>
660:             <td>Semua dokumen credential (PDF/image) + metadata disimpan di Walrus. Blob ID on-chain. Revocation check via Walrus fetch.</td>
661:             <td><span class="tag tag-g">20%</span></td>
662:           </tr>
663:           <tr>
664:             <td><strong>Tatum RPC Usage</strong></td>
665:             <td>Semua on-chain call via Tatum endpoint, bukan public RPC lain.</td>
666:             <td>Semua SuiClient dikonfigurasi ke <code>sui-mainnet.gateway.tatum.io</code> dengan API key. Query credential, event, object via Tatum.</td>
667:             <td><span class="tag tag-g">10%</span></td>
668:           </tr>
669:           <tr>
670:             <td><strong>Technical Quality</strong></td>
671:             <td>Clean Move code, successful deployment mainnet, error handling, README lengkap.</td>
672:             <td>Move module terstruktur, unit test, deploy ke Sui Mainnet, CI/CD, TypeScript SDK, error boundaries di frontend.</td>
673:             <td><span class="tag tag-b">30%</span></td>
674:           </tr>
675:           <tr>
676:             <td><strong>Creativity</strong></td>
677:             <td>Unique use case, solves real problem, tidak generik.</td>
678:             <td>Credential verification adalah masalah nyata milyaran orang. WalTrust = LinkedIn versi trustless. Bukan sekadar "todo app di blockchain".</td>
679:             <td><span class="tag tag-a">20%</span></td>
680:           </tr>
681:           <tr>
682:             <td><strong>Presentation</strong></td>
683:             <td>Demo video 2-3 menit yang jelas, README profesional, live demo link.</td>
684:             <td>Script demo sudah direncanakan. Voiceover storytelling. GitHub README dengan arsitektur diagram + setup guide.</td>
685:             <td><span class="tag tag-a">20%</span></td>
686:           </tr>
687:           <tr>
688:             <td><strong>Bonus: Best Walrus</strong></td>
689:             <td>Most creative + effective Walrus use.</td>
690:             <td>Walrus menyimpan PDF credential + revocation status metadata. Blob ID di-store on-chain. Access revocation in 1 tx.</td>
691:             <td><span class="tag tag-g">+$200</span></td>
692:           </tr>
693:           <tr>
694:             <td><strong>Bonus: Best Tatum</strong></td>
695:             <td>Leverage Tatum RPC, Data API, atau MCP.</td>
696:             <td>Tatum RPC untuk semua query. Tatum Data API untuk transaction history. MCP server untuk AI features (opsional).</td>
697:             <td><span class="tag tag-g">+$200</span></td>
698:           </tr>
699:         </tbody>
700:       </table>
701:     </div>
702:

834: <!-- ==================== SECTION 4: SMART CONTRACT ==================== -->
835: <section class="section" id="smart-contract">
836:   <div class="container">
837:     <div class="section-label" data-num="04">SMART CONTRACT</div>
838:     <h2 class="section-title">Move Smart Contract</h2>
839:     <p class="section-desc">Kode lengkap Move module untuk credential issuance, verification, dan revocation. Deploy-ready ke Sui Mainnet.</p>
840: 
841:     <div class="callout callout-blue">
842:       <span class="callout-icon">­¤ÆĪ</span>
843:       <div class="callout-text">
844:         <strong>Move.toml config:</strong> Pastikan <code>[package] published-at</code> diisi setelah deploy mainnet. Ini penting untuk Tatum RPC agar bisa resolve package address dengan benar.
845:       </div>
846:     </div>
847: 
848:     <div class="code-wrap">
849:       <div class="code-header">
850:         <span class="code-file">contracts/Move.toml</span>
851:         <span class="code-desc">Package manifest</span>
852:       </div>
853:       <div class="code-block">
854: <span class="cm"># contracts/Move.toml</span>
855: [<span class="prop">package</span>]
856: <span class="prop">name</span> = <span class="str">"WalTrust"</span>
857: <span class="prop">version</span> = <span class="str">"1.0.0"</span>
858: <span class="prop">edition</span> = <span class="str">"2024.beta"</span>
859: 
860: [<span class="prop">dependencies</span>]
861: <span class="prop">Sui</span> = { <span class="prop">git</span> = <span class="str">"https://github.com/MystenLabs/sui.git"</span>, <span class="prop">subdir</span> = <span class="str">"crates/sui-framework/packages/sui-framework"</span>, <span class="prop">rev</span> = <span class="str">"framework/mainnet"</span> }
862: 
863: [<span class="prop">addresses</span>]
864: <span class="prop">waltrust</span> = <span class="str">"0x0"</span>  <span class="cm"># Will be replaced after deploy</span>
865:       </div>
866:     </div>
867: 
868:     <div class="code-wrap">
869:       <div class="code-header">
870:         <span class="code-file">contracts/sources/credential.move</span>
871:         <span class="code-desc">Core credential module ŌĆö 90% dari nilai Walrus integration ada di sini</span>
872:       </div>
873:       <div class="code-block">
874: <span class="cm">/// WalTrust ŌĆö Decentralized Credential Verification System</span>
875: <span class="cm">/// Stores credential metadata on-chain, documents on Walrus</span>
876: <span class="kw">module</span> <span class="fn">waltrust</span>::<span class="fn">credential</span> {
877:     <span class="kw">use</span> <span class="fn">sui</span>::<span class="fn">object</span>::{<span class="ty">Self</span>, <span class="ty">UID</span>, <span class="ty">ID</span>};
878:     <span class="kw">use</span> <span class="fn">sui</span>::<span class="fn">tx_context</span>::{<span class="ty">Self</span>, <span class="ty">TxContext</span>};
879:     <span class="kw">use</span> <span class="fn">sui</span>::<span class="fn">transfer</span>;
880:     <span class="kw">use</span> <span class="fn">sui</span>::<span class="fn">event</span>;
881:     <span class="kw">use</span> <span class="fn">std</span>::<span class="fn">string</span>::{<span class="ty">Self</span>, <span class="ty">String</span>};
882:     <span class="kw">use</span> <span class="fn">sui</span>::<span class="fn">clock</span>::{<span class="ty">Self</span>, <span class="ty">Clock</span>};
883:     <span class="kw">use</span> <span class="fn">sui</span>::<span class="fn">vec_map</span>::{<span class="ty">Self</span>, <span class="ty">VecMap</span>};
884: 
885:     <span class="cm">// ============ STRUCTS ============</span>
886: 
887:     <span class="cm">/// Main credential object ŌĆö transferable NFT</span>
888:     <span class="kw">public</span> <span class="kw">struct</span> <span class="ty">Credential</span> <span class="kw">has</span> <span class="ty">key</span>, <span class="ty">store</span> {
889:         <span class="prop">id</span>: <span class="ty">UID</span>,
890:         <span class="cm">/// Walrus Blob ID ŌĆö dokumen asli tersimpan di sini</span>
891:         <span class="prop">walrus_blob_id</span>: <span class="ty">String</span>,
892:         <span class="cm">/// Walrus Blob ID untuk metadata JSON</span>
893:         <span class="prop">walrus_metadata_blob_id</span>: <span class="ty">String</span>,
894:         <span class="cm">/// Hash SHA-256 dari dokumen (verification layer kedua)</span>
895:         <span class="prop">document_hash</span>: <span class="ty">vector</span>&lt;<span class="ty">u8</span>&gt;,
896:         <span class="cm">/// Tipe credential: "degree" | "certificate" | "work_experience"</span>
897:         <span class="prop">credential_type</span>: <span class="ty">String</span>,
898:         <span class="cm">/// Nama credential (e.g., "S1 Teknik Informatika")</span>
899:         <span class="prop">title</span>: <span class="ty">String</span>,
900:         <span class="cm">/// Institusi penerbit (address)</span>
901:         <span class="prop">issuer</span>: <span class="ty">address</span>,
902:         <span class="cm">/// Nama institusi (display)</span>
903:         <span class="prop">issuer_name</span>: <span class="ty">String</span>,
904:         <span class="cm">/// Penerima credential</span>
905:         <span class="prop">recipient</span>: <span class="ty">address</span>,
906:         <span class="cm">/// Nama penerima</span>
907:         <span class="prop">recipient_name</span>: <span class="ty">String</span>,
908:         <span class="cm">/// Tanggal issued (Unix timestamp ms)</span>
909:         <span class="prop">issued_at</span>: <span class="ty">u64</span>,
910:         <span class="cm">/// Tanggal expired (0 = tidak expired)</span>
911:         <span class="prop">expires_at</span>: <span class="ty">u64</span>,
912:         <span class="cm">/// Status: true = valid, false = revoked</span>
913:         <span class="prop">is_valid</span>: <span class="ty">bool</span>,
914:         <span class="cm">/// Extra fields untuk extensibility</span>
915:         <span class="prop">extra_fields</span>: <span class="ty">VecMap</span>&lt;<span class="ty">String</span>, <span class="ty">String</span>&gt;,
916:     }
917: 
918:     <span class="cm">/// Capability untuk issuer yang terverifikasi</span>
919:     <span class="kw">public</span> <span class="kw">struct</span> <span class="ty">IssuerCap</span> <span class="kw">has</span> <span class="ty">key</span>, <span class="ty">store</span> {
920:         <span class="prop">id</span>: <span class="ty">UID</span>,
921:         <span class="prop">issuer_address</span>: <span class="ty">address</span>,
922:         <span class="prop">issuer_name</span>: <span class="ty">String</span>,
923:         <span class="prop">is_active</span>: <span class="ty">bool</span>,
924:     }
925: 
926:     <span class="cm">/// Admin capability untuk mengelola issuer registry</span>
927:     <span class="kw">public</span> <span class="kw">struct</span> <span class="ty">AdminCap</span> <span class="kw">has</span> <span class="ty">key</span>, <span class="ty">store</span> {
928:         <span class="prop">id</span>: <span class="ty">UID</span>,
929:     }
930: 
931:     <span class="cm">// ============ EVENTS ============</span>
932: 
933:     <span class="kw">public</span> <span class="kw">struct</span> <span class="ty">CredentialIssued</span> <span class="kw">has</span> <span class="ty">copy</span>, <span class="ty">drop</span> {
934:         <span class="prop">credential_id</span>: <span class="ty">ID</span>,
935:         <span class="prop">issuer</span>: <span class="ty">address</span>,
936:         <span class="prop">recipient</span>: <span class="ty">address</span>,
937:         <span class="prop">walrus_blob_id</span>: <span class="ty">String</span>,
938:         <span class="prop">credential_type</span>: <span class="ty">String</span>,
939:         <span class="prop">issued_at</span>: <span class="ty">u64</span>,
940:     }
941: 
942:     <span class="kw">public</span> <span class="kw">struct</span> <span class="ty">CredentialRevoked</span> <span class="kw">has</span> <span class="ty">copy</span>, <span class="ty">drop</span> {
943:         <span class="prop">credential_id</span>: <span class="ty">ID</span>,
944:         <span class="prop">revoked_by</span>: <span class="ty">address</span>,
945:         <span class="prop">revoked_at</span>: <span class="ty">u64</span>,
946:     }
947: 
948:     <span class="kw">public</span> <span class="kw">struct</span> <span class="ty">CredentialVerified</span> <span class="kw">has</span> <span class="ty">copy</span>, <span class="ty">drop</span> {
949:         <span class="prop">credential_id</span>: <span class="ty">ID</span>,
950:         <span class="prop">verifier</span>: <span class="ty">address</span>,
951:         <span class="prop">is_valid</span>: <span class="ty">bool</span>,
952:         <span class="prop">verified_at</span>: <span class="ty">u64</span>,
953:     }
954: 
955:     <span class="cm">// ============ INIT ============</span>
956: 
957:     <span class="kw">fun</span> <span class="fn">init</span>(<span class="prop">ctx</span>: &<span class="kw">mut</span> <span class="ty">TxContext</span>) {
958:         <span class="cm">// Transfer AdminCap ke deployer</span>
959:         <span class="kw">let</span> <span class="prop">admin_cap</span> = <span class="ty">AdminCap</span> {
960:             <span class="prop">id</span>: <span class="fn">object</span>::<span class="fn">new</span>(<span class="prop">ctx</span>),
961:         };
962:         <span class="fn">transfer</span>::<span class="fn">transfer</span>(<span class="prop">admin_cap</span>, <span class="fn">tx_context</span>::<span class="fn">sender</span>(<span class="prop">ctx</span>));
963:     }
964: 
965:     <span class="cm">// ============ PUBLIC ENTRY FUNCTIONS ============</span>
966: 
967:     <span class="cm">/// Issue credential baru ŌĆö hanya IssuerCap holder yang bisa</span>
968:     <span class="kw">public</span> <span class="kw">entry</span> <span class="kw">fun</span> <span class="fn">issue_credential</span>(
969:         <span class="prop">issuer_cap</span>: &<span class="ty">IssuerCap</span>,
970:         <span class="prop">walrus_blob_id</span>: <span class="ty">vector</span>&lt;<span class="ty">u8</span>&gt;,
971:         <span class="prop">walrus_metadata_blob_id</span>: <span class="ty">vector</span>&lt;<span class="ty">u8</span>&gt;,
972:         <span class="prop">document_hash</span>: <span class="ty">vector</span>&lt;<span class="ty">u8</span>&gt;,
973:         <span class="prop">credential_type</span>: <span class="ty">vector</span>&lt;<span class="ty">u8</span>&gt;,
974:         <span class="prop">title</span>: <span class="ty">vector</span>&lt;<span class="ty">u8</span>&gt;,
975:         <span class="prop">recipient</span>: <span class="ty">address</span>,
976:         <span class="prop">recipient_name</span>: <span class="ty">vector</span>&lt;<span class="ty">u8</span>&gt;,
977:         <span class="prop">expires_at</span>: <span class="ty">u64</span>,
978:         <span class="prop">clock</span>: &<span class="ty">Clock</span>,
979:         <span class="prop">ctx</span>: &<span class="kw">mut</span> <span class="ty">TxContext</span>
980:     ) {
981:         <span class="fn">assert!</span>(<span class="prop">issuer_cap</span>.<span class="prop">is_active</span>, <span class="num">1001</span>); <span class="cm">// E_ISSUER_NOT_ACTIVE</span>
982: 
983:         <span class="kw">let</span> <span class="prop">issued_at</span> = <span class="fn">clock</span>::<span class="fn">timestamp_ms</span>(<span class="prop">clock</span>);
984:         <span class="kw">let</span> <span class="prop">credential_id</span> = <span class="fn">object</span>::<span class="fn">new</span>(<span class="prop">ctx</span>);
985:         <span class="kw">let</span> <span class="prop">cred_obj_id</span> = <span class="fn">object</span>::<span class="fn">uid_to_inner</span>(&<span class="prop">credential_id</span>);
986: 
987:         <span class="kw">let</span> <span class="prop">credential</span> = <span class="ty">Credential</span> {
988:             <span class="prop">id</span>: <span class="prop">credential_id</span>,
989:             <span class="prop">walrus_blob_id</span>: <span class="fn">string</span>::<span class="fn">utf8</span>(<span class="prop">walrus_blob_id</span>),
990:             <span class="prop">walrus_metadata_blob_id</span>: <span class="fn">string</span>::<span class="fn">utf8</span>(<span class="prop">walrus_metadata_blob_id</span>),
991:             <span class="prop">document_hash</span>,
992:             <span class="prop">credential_type</span>: <span class="fn">string</span>::<span class="fn">utf8</span>(<span class="prop">credential_type</span>),
993:             <span class="prop">title</span>: <span class="fn">string</span>::<span class="fn">utf8</span>(<span class="prop">title</span>),
994:             <span class="prop">issuer</span>: <span class="prop">issuer_cap</span>.<span class="prop">issuer_address</span>,
995:             <span class="prop">issuer_name</span>: <span class="prop">issuer_cap</span>.<span class="prop">issuer_name</span>,
996:             <span class="prop">recipient</span>,
997:             <span class="prop">recipient_name</span>: <span class="fn">string</span>::<span class="fn">utf8</span>(<span class="prop">recipient_name</span>),
998:             <span class="prop">issued_at</span>,
999:             <span class="prop">expires_at</span>,
1000:             <span class="prop">is_valid</span>: <span class="kw">true</span>,
1001:             <span class="prop">extra_fields</span>: <span class="fn">vec_map</span>::<span class="fn">empty</span>(),
1002:         };
1003: 
1004:         <span class="cm">// Emit event ŌĆö Tatum Data API bisa subscribe ke ini</span>
1005:         <span class="fn">event</span>::<span class="fn">emit</span>(<span class="ty">CredentialIssued</span> {
1006:             <span class="prop">credential_id</span>: <span class="prop">cred_obj_id</span>,
1007:             <span class="prop">issuer</span>: <span class="prop">issuer_cap</span>.<span class="prop">issuer_address</span>,
1008:             <span class="prop">recipient</span>,
1009:             <span class="prop">walrus_blob_id</span>: <span class="prop">credential</span>.<span class="prop">walrus_blob_id</span>,
1010:             <span class="prop">credential_type</span>: <span class="prop">credential</span>.<span class="prop">credential_type</span>,
1011:             <span class="prop">issued_at</span>,
1012:         });
1013: 
1014:         <span class="cm">// Transfer credential ke recipient</span>
1015:         <span class="fn">transfer</span>::<span class="fn">transfer</span>(<span class="prop">credential</span>, <span class="prop">recipient</span>);
1016:     }
1017: 
1018:     <span class="cm">/// Revoke credential ŌĆö hanya issuer asli yang bisa</span>
1019:     <span class="kw">public</span> <span class="kw">entry</span> <span class="kw">fun</span> <span class="fn">revoke_credential</span>(
1020:         <span class="prop">issuer_cap</span>: &<span class="ty">IssuerCap</span>,
1021:         <span class="prop">credential</span>: &<span class="kw">mut</span> <span class="ty">Credential</span>,
1022:         <span class="prop">clock</span>: &<span class="ty">Clock</span>,
1023:         <span class="prop">ctx</span>: &<span class="kw">mut</span> <span class="ty">TxContext</span>
1024:     ) {
1025:         <span class="fn">assert!</span>(<span class="prop">issuer_cap</span>.<span class="prop">issuer_address</span> == <span class="prop">credential</span>.<span class="prop">issuer</span>, <span class="num">1002</span>);
1026:         <span class="fn">assert!</span>(<span class="prop">credential</span>.<span class="prop">is_valid</span>, <span class="num">1003</span>); <span class="cm">// Already revoked</span>
1027: 
1028:         <span class="prop">credential</span>.<span class="prop">is_valid</span> = <span class="kw">false</span>;
1029: 
1030:         <span class="fn">event</span>::<span class="fn">emit</span>(<span class="ty">CredentialRevoked</span> {
1031:             <span class="prop">credential_id</span>: <span class="fn">object</span>::<span class="fn">uid_to_inner</span>(&<span class="prop">credential</span>.<span class="prop">id</span>),
1032:             <span class="prop">revoked_by</span>: <span class="fn">tx_context</span>::<span class="fn">sender</span>(<span class="prop">ctx</span>),
1033:             <span class="prop">revoked_at</span>: <span class="fn">clock</span>::<span class="fn">timestamp_ms</span>(<span class="prop">clock</span>),
1034:         });
1035:     }
1036: 
1037:     <span class="cm">/// Public verify ŌĆö siapa saja bisa query status credential</span>
1038:     <span class="kw">public</span> <span class="kw">fun</span> <span class="fn">verify_credential</span>(
1039:         <span class="prop">credential</span>: &<span class="ty">Credential</span>,
1040:         <span class="prop">clock</span>: &<span class="ty">Clock</span>,
1041:         <span class="prop">ctx</span>: &<span class="kw">mut</span> <span class="ty">TxContext</span>
1042:     ): <span class="ty">bool</span> {
1043:         <span class="kw">let</span> <span class="prop">now</span> = <span class="fn">clock</span>::<span class="fn">timestamp_ms</span>(<span class="prop">clock</span>);
1044:         <span class="kw">let</span> <span class="prop">not_expired</span> = <span class="prop">credential</span>.<span class="prop">expires_at</span> == <span class="num">0</span> || <span class="prop">now</span> &lt; <span class="prop">credential</span>.<span class="prop">expires_at</span>;
1045:         <span class="kw">let</span> <span class="prop">is_valid</span> = <span class="prop">credential</span>.<span class="prop">is_valid</span> &amp;&amp; <span class="prop">not_expired</span>;
1046: 
1047:         <span class="fn">event</span>::<span class="fn">emit</span>(<span class="ty">CredentialVerified</span> {
1048:             <span class="prop">credential_id</span>: <span class="fn">object</span>::<span class="fn">uid_to_inner</span>(&<span class="prop">credential</span>.<span class="prop">id</span>),
1049:             <span class="prop">verifier</span>: <span class="fn">tx_context</span>::<span class="fn">sender</span>(<span class="prop">ctx</span>),
1050:             <span class="prop">is_valid</span>,
1051:             <span class="prop">verified_at</span>: <span class="prop">now</span>,
1052:         });
1053:         <span class="prop">is_valid</span>
1054:     }
1055: 
1056:     <span class="cm">// ============ VIEW FUNCTIONS ============</span>
1057: 
1058:     <span class="kw">public</span> <span class="kw">fun</span> <span class="fn">get_walrus_blob_id</span>(<span class="prop">c</span>: &<span class="ty">Credential</span>): &<span class="ty">String</span> { &<span class="prop">c</span>.<span class="prop">walrus_blob_id</span> }
1059:     <span class="kw">public</span> <span class="kw">fun</span> <span class="fn">get_issuer</span>(<span class="prop">c</span>: &<span class="ty">Credential</span>): <span class="ty">address</span> { <span class="prop">c</span>.<span class="prop">issuer</span> }
1060:     <span class="kw">public</span> <span class="kw">fun</span> <span class="fn">get_recipient</span>(<span class="prop">c</span>: &<span class="ty">Credential</span>): <span class="ty">address</span> { <span class="prop">c</span>.<span class="prop">recipient</span> }
1061:     <span class="kw">public</span> <span class="kw">fun</span> <span class="fn">is_valid</span>(<span class="prop">c</span>: &<span class="ty">Credential</span>): <span class="ty">bool</span> { <span class="prop">c</span>.<span class="prop">is_valid</span> }
1062:     <span class="kw">public</span> <span class="kw">fun</span> <span class="fn">get_document_hash</span>(<span class="prop">c</span>: &<span class="ty">Credential</span>): &<span class="ty">vector</span>&lt;<span class="ty">u8</span>&gt; { &<span class="prop">c</span>.<span class="prop">document_hash</span> }
1063: }
1064:       </div>
1065:     </div>
1066: 
1067:     <div class="code-wrap">
1068:       <div class="code-header">
1069:         <span class="code-file">contracts/sources/issuer.move</span>
1070:         <span class="code-desc">Issuer registry ŌĆö admin approve issuer resmi</span>
1071:       </div>
1072:       <div class="code-block">
1073: <span class="kw">module</span> <span class="fn">waltrust</span>::<span class="fn">issuer</span> {
1074:     <span class="kw">use</span> <span class="fn">waltrust</span>::<span class="fn">credential</span>::{<span class="ty">AdminCap</span>, <span class="ty">IssuerCap</span>};
1075:     <span class="kw">use</span> <span class="fn">sui</span>::<span class="fn">object</span>::{<span class="ty">Self</span>, <span class="ty">UID</span>};
1076:     <span class="kw">use</span> <span class="fn">sui</span>::<span class="fn">transfer</span>;
1077:     <span class="kw">use</span> <span class="fn">sui</span>::<span class="fn">tx_context</span>::<span class="ty">TxContext</span>;
1078:     <span class="kw">use</span> <span class="fn">std</span>::<span class="fn">string</span>;
1079: 
1080:     <span class="cm">/// Admin approve issuer baru (universitas, lembaga sertifikasi)</span>
1081:     <span class="kw">public</span> <span class="kw">entry</span> <span class="kw">fun</span> <span class="fn">approve_issuer</span>(
1082:         <span class="prop">_admin</span>: &<span class="ty">AdminCap</span>,
1083:         <span class="prop">issuer_address</span>: <span class="ty">address</span>,
1084:         <span class="prop">issuer_name</span>: <span class="ty">vector</span>&lt;<span class="ty">u8</span>&gt;,
1085:         <span class="prop">ctx</span>: &<span class="kw">mut</span> <span class="ty">TxContext</span>
1086:     ) {
1087:         <span class="kw">let</span> <span class="prop">cap</span> = <span class="ty">IssuerCap</span> {
1088:             <span class="prop">id</span>: <span class="fn">object</span>::<span class="fn">new</span>(<span class="prop">ctx</span>),
1089:             <span class="prop">issuer_address</span>,
1090:             <span class="prop">issuer_name</span>: <span class="fn">string</span>::<span class="fn">utf8</span>(<span class="prop">issuer_name</span>),
1091:             <span class="prop">is_active</span>: <span class="kw">true</span>,
1092:         };
1093:         <span class="fn">transfer</span>::<span class="fn">transfer</span>(<span class="prop">cap</span>, <span class="prop">issuer_address</span>);
1094:     }
1095: }
1096:       </div>

1103:       </div>

1106: <span class="op">sui</span> client switch --env mainnet
1107: 
1108: <span class="cm"># 2. Build & verify</span>
1109: <span class="op">sui</span> move build --skip-fetch-latest-git-deps
1110: 
1111: <span class="cm"># 3. Test sebelum deploy</span>
1112: <span class="op">sui</span> move test
1113: 
1114: <span class="cm"># 4. Deploy ke Mainnet</span>
1115: <span class="op">sui</span> client publish \
1116:   --gas-budget <span class="num">100000000</span> \
1117:   --json
1118: 
1119: <span class="cm"># 5. Simpan package ID dari output:</span>
1120: <span class="cm"># "packageId": "0x..." ŌåÆ masuk ke .env</span>
1121: <span class="cm"># "objectId" AdminCap ŌåÆ simpan untuk approve issuer</span>

1126: 
1127: <!-- ==================== SECTION 5: WALRUS ==================== -->
1128: <section class="section" id="walrus">
1129:   <div class="container">
1130:     <div class="section-label" data-num="05">WALRUS INTEGRATION</div>
1131:     <h2 class="section-title">Walrus Storage Layer</h2>
1132:     <p class="section-desc">Cara WalTrust menggunakan Walrus sebagai core storage ŌĆö bukan add-on. Ini adalah kunci untuk memenangkan bonus "Best Walrus Integration" senilai $200.</p>
1133: 
1134:     <div class="callout callout-green">
1135:       <span class="callout-icon">­¤Åå</span>
1136:       <div class="callout-text">
1137:         <strong>Winning formula Walrus:</strong> Simpan 2 blobs per credential ŌĆö (1) dokumen asli PDF/image, (2) metadata JSON. Blob ID keduanya di-store on-chain di SUI. Ini membuktikan <em>meaningful integration</em> yang juri cari.
1138:       </div>
1139:     </div>
1140: 
1141:     <h3>Walrus Endpoints</h3>
1142:     <div class="table-wrap">
1143:       <table>
1144:         <thead><tr><th>Endpoint</th><th>URL</th><th>Digunakan untuk</th></tr></thead>
1145:         <tbody>
1146:           <tr><td><strong>Publisher (Mainnet)</strong></td><td><code>https://publisher.walrus-mainnet.walrus.space</code></td><td>Upload dokumen credential</td></tr>
1147:           <tr><td><strong>Aggregator (Mainnet)</strong></td><td><code>https://aggregator.walrus-mainnet.walrus.space</code></td><td>Fetch dokumen untuk display</td></tr>
1148:           <tr><td><strong>Publisher (Testnet)</strong></td><td><code>https://publisher.walrus-testnet.walrus.space</code></td><td>Development & testing</td></tr>
1149:           <tr><td><strong>Aggregator (Testnet)</strong></td><td><code>https://aggregator.walrus-testnet.walrus.space</code></td><td>Development & testing</td></tr>
1150:         </tbody>
1151:       </table>
1152:     </div>
1153: 
1154:     <div class="code-wrap">
1155:       <div class="code-header">
1156:         <span class="code-file">app/lib/walrus.ts</span>
1157:         <span class="code-desc">Complete Walrus upload + fetch helper</span>
1158:       </div>
1159:       <div class="code-block">
1160: <span class="cm">// app/lib/walrus.ts</span>
1161: <span class="kw">const</span> <span class="prop">WALRUS_PUBLISHER</span> = <span class="str">"https://publisher.walrus-mainnet.walrus.space"</span>;
1162: <span class="kw">const</span> <span class="prop">WALRUS_AGGREGATOR</span> = <span class="str">"https://aggregator.walrus-mainnet.walrus.space"</span>;
1163: <span class="kw">const</span> <span class="prop">STORAGE_EPOCHS</span> = <span class="num">365</span>; <span class="cm">// ~1 tahun</span>
1164: 
1165: <span class="kw">export interface</span> <span class="ty">WalrusUploadResult</span> {
1166:   <span class="prop">blobId</span>: <span class="ty">string</span>;
1167:   <span class="prop">suiObjectId</span>: <span class="ty">string</span>;
1168:   <span class="prop">endEpoch</span>: <span class="ty">number</span>;
1169:   <span class="prop">isNewlyCreated</span>: <span class="ty">boolean</span>;
1170: }
1171: 
1172: <span class="kw">export interface</span> <span class="ty">CredentialMetadata</span> {
1173:   <span class="prop">title</span>: <span class="ty">string</span>;
1174:   <span class="prop">credentialType</span>: <span class="ty">string</span>;
1175:   <span class="prop">issuerName</span>: <span class="ty">string</span>;
1176:   <span class="prop">recipientName</span>: <span class="ty">string</span>;
1177:   <span class="prop">issuedAt</span>: <span class="ty">string</span>; <span class="cm">// ISO date</span>
1178:   <span class="prop">expiresAt</span>: <span class="ty">string</span> | <span class="kw">null</span>;
1179:   <span class="prop">additionalInfo</span>: <span class="ty">Record</span>&lt;<span class="ty">string</span>, <span class="ty">string</span>&gt;;
1180: }
1181: 
1182: <span class="cm">/**
1183:  * Upload file blob ke Walrus
1184:  * Returns blob ID yang akan disimpan on-chain di SUI
1185:  */</span>
1186: <span class="kw">export async function</span> <span class="fn">uploadToWalrus</span>(
1187:   <span class="prop">fileData</span>: <span class="ty">Uint8Array</span> | <span class="ty">Blob</span>,
1188:   <span class="prop">contentType</span>: <span class="ty">string</span> = <span class="str">"application/octet-stream"</span>
1189: ): <span class="ty">Promise</span>&lt;<span class="ty">WalrusUploadResult</span>&gt; {
1190:   <span class="kw">const</span> <span class="prop">response</span> = <span class="kw">await</span> <span class="fn">fetch</span>(
1191:     <span class="str">`</span><span class="prop">${WALRUS_PUBLISHER}</span><span class="str">/v1/blobs?epochs=</span><span class="prop">${STORAGE_EPOCHS}</span><span class="str">`</span>,
1192:     {
1193:       <span class="prop">method</span>: <span class="str">"PUT"</span>,
1194:       <span class="prop">headers</span>: { <span class="str">"Content-Type"</span>: <span class="prop">contentType</span> },
1195:       <span class="prop">body</span>: <span class="prop">fileData</span>,
1196:     }
1197:   );
1198: 
1199:   <span class="kw">if</span> (!<span class="prop">response</span>.<span class="prop">ok</span>) {
1200:     <span class="kw">throw new</span> <span class="fn">Error</span>(<span class="str">`Walrus upload failed: </span><span class="prop">${response.status}</span><span class="str">`</span>);
1201:   }
1202: 
1203:   <span class="kw">const</span> <span class="prop">result</span> = <span class="kw">await</span> <span class="prop">response</span>.<span class="fn">json</span>();
1204: 
1205:   <span class="cm">// Handle both newlyCreated and alreadyCertified responses</span>
1206:   <span class="kw">if</span> (<span class="prop">result</span>.<span class="prop">newlyCreated</span>) {
1207:     <span class="kw">return</span> {
1208:       <span class="prop">blobId</span>: <span class="prop">result</span>.<span class="prop">newlyCreated</span>.<span class="prop">blobObject</span>.<span class="prop">blobId</span>,
1209:       <span class="prop">suiObjectId</span>: <span class="prop">result</span>.<span class="prop">newlyCreated</span>.<span class="prop">blobObject</span>.<span class="prop">id</span>,
1210:       <span class="prop">endEpoch</span>: <span class="prop">result</span>.<span class="prop">newlyCreated</span>.<span class="prop">blobObject</span>.<span class="prop">storage</span>.<span class="prop">endEpoch</span>,
1211:       <span class="prop">isNewlyCreated</span>: <span class="kw">true</span>,
1212:     };
1213:   } <span class="kw">else if</span> (<span class="prop">result</span>.<span class="prop">alreadyCertified</span>) {
1214:     <span class="kw">return</span> {
1215:       <span class="prop">blobId</span>: <span class="prop">result</span>.<span class="prop">alreadyCertified</span>.<span class="prop">blobId</span>,
1216:       <span class="prop">suiObjectId</span>: <span class="str">""</span>,
1217:       <span class="prop">endEpoch</span>: <span class="prop">result</span>.<span class="prop">alreadyCertified</span>.<span class="prop">endEpoch</span>,
1218:       <span class="prop">isNewlyCreated</span>: <span class="kw">false</span>,
1219:     };
1220:   }
1221: 
1222:   <span class="kw">throw new</span> <span class="fn">Error</span>(<span class="str">"Unexpected Walrus response format"</span>);
1223: }
1224: 
1225: <span class="cm">/**
1226:  * Upload metadata JSON ke Walrus
1227:  * Metadata berisi info credential yang bisa dibaca tanpa buka PDF
1228:  */</span>
1229: <span class="kw">export async function</span> <span class="fn">uploadMetadataToWalrus</span>(
1230:   <span class="prop">metadata</span>: <span class="ty">CredentialMetadata</span>
1231: ): <span class="ty">Promise</span>&lt;<span class="ty">WalrusUploadResult</span>&gt; {
1232:   <span class="kw">const</span> <span class="prop">jsonBytes</span> = <span class="kw">new</span> <span class="fn">TextEncoder</span>().<span class="fn">encode</span>(<span class="fn">JSON</span>.<span class="fn">stringify</span>(<span class="prop">metadata</span>));
1233:   <span class="kw">return</span> <span class="fn">uploadToWalrus</span>(<span class="prop">jsonBytes</span>, <span class="str">"application/json"</span>);
1234: }
1235: 
1236: <span class="cm">/**
1237:  * Fetch blob dari Walrus by Blob ID
1238:  * Digunakan di verifier page untuk tampilkan dokumen
1239:  */</span>
1240: <span class="kw">export async function</span> <span class="fn">fetchFromWalrus</span>(<span class="prop">blobId</span>: <span class="ty">string</span>): <span class="ty">Promise</span>&lt;<span class="ty">Blob</span>&gt; {
1241:   <span class="kw">const</span> <span class="prop">response</span> = <span class="kw">await</span> <span class="fn">fetch</span>(
1242:     <span class="str">`</span><span class="prop">${WALRUS_AGGREGATOR}</span><span class="str">/v1/blobs/</span><span class="prop">${blobId}</span><span class="str">`</span>
1243:   );
1244: 
1245:   <span class="kw">if</span> (!<span class="prop">response</span>.<span class="prop">ok</span>) {
1246:     <span class="kw">throw new</span> <span class="fn">Error</span>(<span class="str">`Walrus fetch failed for blob: </span><span class="prop">${blobId}</span><span class="str">`</span>);
1247:   }
1248: 
1249:   <span class="kw">return</span> <span class="prop">response</span>.<span class="fn">blob</span>();
1250: }
1251: 
1252: <span class="cm">/**
1253:  * Fetch metadata JSON dari Walrus
1254:  */</span>
1255: <span class="kw">export async function</span> <span class="fn">fetchMetadataFromWalrus</span>(
1256:   <span class="prop">metadataBlobId</span>: <span class="ty">string</span>
1257: ): <span class="ty">Promise</span>&lt;<span class="ty">CredentialMetadata</span>&gt; {
1258:   <span class="kw">const</span> <span class="prop">blob</span> = <span class="kw">await</span> <span class="fn">fetchFromWalrus</span>(<span class="prop">metadataBlobId</span>);
1259:   <span class="kw">const</span> <span class="prop">text</span> = <span class="kw">await</span> <span class="prop">blob</span>.<span class="fn">text</span>();
1260:   <span class="kw">return</span> <span class="fn">JSON</span>.<span class="fn">parse</span>(<span class="prop">text</span>) <span class="kw">as</span> <span class="ty">CredentialMetadata</span>;
1261: }
1262: 
1263: <span class="cm">/**
1264:  * Compute SHA-256 hash dari file (untuk on-chain verification)
1265:  */</span>
1266: <span class="kw">export async function</span> <span class="fn">hashFile</span>(<span class="prop">fileData</span>: <span class="ty">ArrayBuffer</span>): <span class="ty">Promise</span>&lt;<span class="ty">Uint8Array</span>&gt; {
1267:   <span class="kw">const</span> <span class="prop">hashBuffer</span> = <span class="kw">await</span> <span class="prop">crypto</span>.<span class="prop">subtle</span>.<span class="fn">digest</span>(<span class="str">"SHA-256"</span>, <span class="prop">fileData</span>);
1268:   <span class="kw">return new</span> <span class="fn">Uint8Array</span>(<span class="prop">hashBuffer</span>);
1269: }
1270:       </div>

905:         <span class="prop">recipient</span>: <span class="ty">address</span>,
906:         <span class="cm">/// Nama penerima</span>
907:         <span class="prop">recipient_name</span>: <span class="ty">String</span>,
908:         <span class="cm">/// Tanggal issued (Unix timestamp ms)</span>
909:         <span class="prop">issued_at</span>: <span class="ty">u64</span>,
910:         <span class="cm">/// Tanggal expired (0 = tidak expired)</span>
911:         <span class="prop">expires_at</span>: <span class="ty">u64</span>,
912:         <span class="cm">/// Status: true = valid, false = revoked</span>
913:         <span class="prop">is_valid</span>: <span class="ty">bool</span>,
914:         <span class="cm">/// Extra fields untuk extensibility</span>
915:         <span class="prop">extra_fields</span>: <span class="ty">VecMap</span>&lt;<span class="ty">String</span>, <span class="ty">String</span>&gt;,
916:     }
917: 
918:     <span class="cm">/// Capability untuk issuer yang terverifikasi</span>
919:     <span class="kw">public</span> <span class="kw">struct</span> <span class="ty">IssuerCap</span> <span class="kw">has</span> <span class="ty">key</span>, <span class="ty">store</span> {
920:         <span class="prop">id</span>: <span class="ty">UID</span>,
921:         <span class="prop">issuer_address</span>: <span class="ty">address</span>,
922:         <span class="prop">issuer_name</span>: <span class="ty">String</span>,
923:         <span class="prop">is_active</span>: <span class="ty">bool</span>,
924:     }
925: 
926:     <span class="cm">/// Admin capability untuk mengelola issuer registry</span>
927:     <span class="kw">public</span> <span class="kw">struct</span> <span class="ty">AdminCap</span> <span class="kw">has</span> <span class="ty">key</span>, <span class="ty">store</span> {
928:         <span class="prop">id</span>: <span class="ty">UID</span>,
929:     }
930: 
931:     <span class="cm">// ============ EVENTS ============</span>
932: 
933:     <span class="kw">public</span> <span class="kw">struct</span> <span class="ty">CredentialIssued</span> <span class="kw">has</span> <span class="ty">copy</span>, <span class="ty">drop</span> {
934:         <span class="prop">credential_id</span>: <span class="ty">ID</span>,
935:         <span class="prop">issuer</span>: <span class="ty">address</span>,
936:         <span class="prop">recipient</span>: <span class="ty">address</span>,
937:         <span class="prop">walrus_blob_id</span>: <span class="ty">String</span>,
938:         <span class="prop">credential_type</span>: <span class="ty">String</span>,
939:         <span class="prop">issued_at</span>: <span class="ty">u64</span>,
940:     }
941: 
942:     <span class="kw">public</span> <span class="kw">struct</span> <span class="ty">CredentialRevoked</span> <span class="kw">has</span> <span class="ty">copy</span>, <span class="ty">drop</span> {
943:         <span class="prop">credential_id</span>: <span class="ty">ID</span>,
944:         <span class="prop">revoked_by</span>: <span class="ty">address</span>,
945:         <span class="prop">revoked_at</span>: <span class="ty">u64</span>,
946:     }
947: 
948:     <span class="kw">public</span> <span class="kw">struct</span> <span class="ty">CredentialVerified</span> <span class="kw">has</span> <span class="ty">copy</span>, <span class="ty">drop</span> {
949:         <span class="prop">credential_id</span>: <span class="ty">ID</span>,
950:         <span class="prop">verifier</span>: <span class="ty">address</span>,
951:         <span class="prop">is_valid</span>: <span class="ty">bool</span>,
952:         <span class="prop">verified_at</span>: <span class="ty">u64</span>,
953:     }
954: 
955:     <span class="cm">// ============ INIT ============</span>
956: 
957:     <span class="kw">fun</span> <span class="fn">init</span>(<span class="prop">ctx</span>: &<span class="kw">mut</span> <span class="ty">TxContext</span>) {
958:         <span class="cm">// Transfer AdminCap ke deployer</span>
959:         <span class="kw">let</span> <span class="prop">admin_cap</span> = <span class="ty">AdminCap</span> {
960:             <span class="prop">id</span>: <span class="fn">object</span>::<span class="fn">new</span>(<span class="prop">ctx</span>),
961:         };
962:         <span class="fn">transfer</span>::<span class="fn">transfer</span>(<span class="prop">admin_cap</span>, <span class="fn">tx_context</span>::<span class="fn">sender</span>(<span class="prop">ctx</span>));
963:     }
964: 
965:     <span class="cm">// ============ PUBLIC ENTRY FUNCTIONS ============</span>
966: 
967:     <span class="cm">/// Issue credential baru ŌĆö hanya IssuerCap holder yang bisa</span>
968:     <span class="kw">public</span> <span class="kw">entry</span> <span class="kw">fun</span> <span class="fn">issue_credential</span>(
969:         <span class="prop">issuer_cap</span>: &<span class="ty">IssuerCap</span>,
970:         <span class="prop">walrus_blob_id</span>: <span class="ty">vector</span>&lt;<span class="ty">u8</span>&gt;,
971:         <span class="prop">walrus_metadata_blob_id</span>: <span class="ty">vector</span>&lt;<span class="ty">u8</span>&gt;,
972:         <span class="prop">document_hash</span>: <span class="ty">vector</span>&lt;<span class="ty">u8</span>&gt;,
973:         <span class="prop">credential_type</span>: <span class="ty">vector</span>&lt;<span class="ty">u8</span>&gt;,
974:         <span class="prop">title</span>: <span class="ty">vector</span>&lt;<span class="ty">u8</span>&gt;,
975:         <span class="prop">recipient</span>: <span class="ty">address</span>,
976:         <span class="prop">recipient_name</span>: <span class="ty">vector</span>&lt;<span class="ty">u8</span>&gt;,
977:         <span class="prop">expires_at</span>: <span class="ty">u64</span>,
978:         <span class="prop">clock</span>: &<span class="ty">Clock</span>,
979:         <span class="prop">ctx</span>: &<span class="kw">mut</span> <span class="ty">TxContext</span>
980:     ) {
981:         <span class="fn">assert!</span>(<span class="prop">issuer_cap</span>.<span class="prop">is_active</span>, <span class="num">1001</span>); <span class="cm">// E_ISSUER_NOT_ACTIVE</span>
982: 
983:         <span class="kw">let</span> <span class="prop">issued_at</span> = <span class="fn">clock</span>::<span class="fn">timestamp_ms</span>(<span class="prop">clock</span>);
984:         <span class="kw">let</span> <span class="prop">credential_id</span> = <span class="fn">object</span>::<span class="fn">new</span>(<span class="prop">ctx</span>);
985:         <span class="kw">let</span> <span class="prop">cred_obj_id</span> = <span class="fn">object</span>::<span class="fn">uid_to_inner</span>(&<span class="prop">credential_id</span>);
986: 
987:         <span class="kw">let</span> <span class="prop">credential</span> = <span class="ty">Credential</span> {
988:             <span class="prop">id</span>: <span class="prop">credential_id</span>,
989:             <span class="prop">walrus_blob_id</span>: <span class="fn">string</span>::<span class="fn">utf8</span>(<span class="prop">walrus_blob_id</span>),
990:             <span class="prop">walrus_metadata_blob_id</span>: <span class="fn">string</span>::<span class="fn">utf8</span>(<span class="prop">walrus_metadata_blob_id</span>),
991:             <span class="prop">document_hash</span>,
992:             <span class="prop">credential_type</span>: <span class="fn">string</span>::<span class="fn">utf8</span>(<span class="prop">credential_type</span>),
993:             <span class="prop">title</span>: <span class="fn">string</span>::<span class="fn">utf8</span>(<span class="prop">title</span>),
994:             <span class="prop">issuer</span>: <span class="prop">issuer_cap</span>.<span class="prop">issuer_address</span>,
995:             <span class="prop">issuer_name</span>: <span class="prop">issuer_cap</span>.<span class="prop">issuer_name</span>,
996:             <span class="prop">recipient</span>,
997:             <span class="prop">recipient_name</span>: <span class="fn">string</span>::<span class="fn">utf8</span>(<span class="prop">recipient_name</span>),
998:             <span class="prop">issued_at</span>,
999:             <span class="prop">expires_at</span>,
1000:             <span class="prop">is_valid</span>: <span class="kw">true</span>,
1001:             <span class="prop">extra_fields</span>: <span class="fn">vec_map</span>::<span class="fn">empty</span>(),
1002:         };
1003: 
1004:         <span class="cm">// Emit event ŌĆö Tatum Data API bisa subscribe ke ini</span>
1005:         <span class="fn">event</span>::<span class="fn">emit</span>(<span class="ty">CredentialIssued</span> {
1006:             <span class="prop">credential_id</span>: <span class="prop">cred_obj_id</span>,
1007:             <span class="prop">issuer</span>: <span class="prop">issuer_cap</span>.<span class="prop">issuer_address</span>,
1008:             <span class="prop">recipient</span>,
1009:             <span class="prop">walrus_blob_id</span>: <span class="prop">credential</span>.<span class="prop">walrus_blob_id</span>,
1010:             <span class="prop">credential_type</span>: <span class="prop">credential</span>.<span class="prop">credential_type</span>,
1011:             <span class="prop">issued_at</span>,
1012:         });
1013: 
1014:         <span class="cm">// Transfer credential ke recipient</span>
1015:         <span class="fn">transfer</span>::<span class="fn">transfer</span>(<span class="prop">credential</span>, <span class="prop">recipient</span>);
1016:     }
1017: 
1018:     <span class="cm">/// Revoke credential ŌĆö hanya issuer asli yang bisa</span>
1019:     <span class="kw">public</span> <span class="kw">entry</span> <span class="kw">fun</span> <span class="fn">revoke_credential</span>(
1020:         <span class="prop">issuer_cap</span>: &<span class="ty">IssuerCap</span>,
1021:         <span class="prop">credential</span>: &<span class="kw">mut</span> <span class="ty">Credential</span>,
1022:         <span class="prop">clock</span>: &<span class="ty">Clock</span>,
1023:         <span class="prop">ctx</span>: &<span class="kw">mut</span> <span class="ty">TxContext</span>
1024:     ) {
1025:         <span class="fn">assert!</span>(<span class="prop">issuer_cap</span>.<span class="prop">issuer_address</span> == <span class="prop">credential</span>.<span class="prop">issuer</span>, <span class="num">1002</span>);
1026:         <span class="fn">assert!</span>(<span class="prop">credential</span>.<span class="prop">is_valid</span>, <span class="num">1003</span>); <span class="cm">// Already revoked</span>
1027: 
1028:         <span class="prop">credential</span>.<span class="prop">is_valid</span> = <span class="kw">false</span>;
1029: 
1030:         <span class="fn">event</span>::<span class="fn">emit</span>(<span class="ty">CredentialRevoked</span> {
1031:             <span class="prop">credential_id</span>: <span class="fn">object</span>::<span class="fn">uid_to_inner</span>(&<span class="prop">credential</span>.<span class="prop">id</span>),
1032:             <span class="prop">revoked_by</span>: <span class="fn">tx_context</span>::<span class="fn">sender</span>(<span class="prop">ctx</span>),
1033:             <span class="prop">revoked_at</span>: <span class="fn">clock</span>::<span class="fn">timestamp_ms</span>(<span class="prop">clock</span>),
1034:         });
1035:     }
1036: 
1037:     <span class="cm">/// Public verify ŌĆö siapa saja bisa query status credential</span>
1038:     <span class="kw">public</span> <span class="kw">fun</span> <span class="fn">verify_credential</span>(
1039:         <span class="prop">credential</span>: &<span class="ty">Credential</span>,
1040:         <span class="prop">clock</span>: &<span class="ty">Clock</span>,
1041:         <span class="prop">ctx</span>: &<span class="kw">mut</span> <span class="ty">TxContext</span>
1042:     ): <span class="ty">bool</span> {
1043:         <span class="kw">let</span> <span class="prop">now</span> = <span class="fn">clock</span>::<span class="fn">timestamp_ms</span>(<span class="prop">clock</span>);
1044:         <span class="kw">let</span> <span class="prop">not_expired</span> = <span class="prop">credential</span>.<span class="prop">expires_at</span> == <span class="num">0</span> || <span class="prop">now</span> &lt; <span class="prop">credential</span>.<span class="prop">expires_at</span>;
1045:         <span class="kw">let</span> <span class="prop">is_valid</span> = <span class="prop">credential</span>.<span class="prop">is_valid</span> &amp;&amp; <span class="prop">not_expired</span>;
1046: 
1047:         <span class="fn">event</span>::<span class="fn">emit</span>(<span class="ty">CredentialVerified</span> {
1048:             <span class="prop">credential_id</span>: <span class="fn">object</span>::<span class="fn">uid_to_inner</span>(&<span class="prop">credential</span>.<span class="prop">id</span>),
1049:             <span class="prop">verifier</span>: <span class="fn">tx_context</span>::<span class="fn">sender</span>(<span class="prop">ctx</span>),
1050:             <span class="prop">is_valid</span>,
1051:             <span class="prop">verified_at</span>: <span class="prop">now</span>,
1052:         });
1053:         <span class="prop">is_valid</span>
1054:     }
1055: 
1056:     <span class="cm">// ============ VIEW FUNCTIONS ============</span>
1057: 
1058:     <span class="kw">public</span> <span class="kw">fun</span> <span class="fn">get_walrus_blob_id</span>(<span class="prop">c</span>: &<span class="ty">Credential</span>): &<span class="ty">String</span> { &<span class="prop">c</span>.<span class="prop">walrus_blob_id</span> }
1059:     <span class="kw">public</span> <span class="kw">fun</span> <span class="fn">get_issuer</span>(<span class="prop">c</span>: &<span class="ty">Credential</span>): <span class="ty">address</span> { <span class="prop">c</span>.<span class="prop">issuer</span> }
1060:     <span class="kw">public</span> <span class="kw">fun</span> <span class="fn">get_recipient</span>(<span class="prop">c</span>: &<span class="ty">Credential</span>): <span class="ty">address</span> { <span class="prop">c</span>.<span class="prop">recipient</span> }
1061:     <span class="kw">public</span> <span class="kw">fun</span> <span class="fn">is_valid</span>(<span class="prop">c</span>: &<span class="ty">Credential</span>): <span class="ty">bool</span> { <span class="prop">c</span>.<span class="prop">is_valid</span> }
1062:     <span class="kw">public</span> <span class="kw">fun</span> <span class="fn">get_document_hash</span>(<span class="prop">c</span>: &<span class="ty">Credential</span>): &<span class="ty">vector</span>&lt;<span class="ty">u8</span>&gt; { &<span class="prop">c</span>.<span class="prop">document_hash</span> }
1063: }
1064:       </div>
1065:     </div>

1073: <span class="kw">module</span> <span class="fn">waltrust</span>::<span class="fn">issuer</span> {
1074:     <span class="kw">use</span> <span class="fn">waltrust</span>::<span class="fn">credential</span>::{<span class="ty">AdminCap</span>, <span class="ty">IssuerCap</span>};
1075:     <span class="kw">use</span> <span class="fn">sui</span>::<span class="fn">object</span>::{<span class="ty">Self</span>, <span class="ty">UID</span>};
1076:     <span class="kw">use</span> <span class="fn">sui</span>::<span class="fn">transfer</span>;
1077:     <span class="kw">use</span> <span class="fn">sui</span>::<span class="fn">tx_context</span>::<span class="ty">TxContext</span>;
1078:     <span class="kw">use</span> <span class="fn">std</span>::<span class="fn">string</span>;
1079: 
1080:     <span class="cm">/// Admin approve issuer baru (universitas, lembaga sertifikasi)</span>
1081:     <span class="kw">public</span> <span class="kw">entry</span> <span class="kw">fun</span> <span class="fn">approve_issuer</span>(
1082:         <span class="prop">_admin</span>: &<span class="ty">AdminCap</span>,
1083:         <span class="prop">issuer_address</span>: <span class="ty">address</span>,
1084:         <span class="prop">issuer_name</span>: <span class="ty">vector</span>&lt;<span class="ty">u8</span>&gt;,
1085:         <span class="prop">ctx</span>: &<span class="kw">mut</span> <span class="ty">TxContext</span>
1086:     ) {
1087:         <span class="kw">let</span> <span class="prop">cap</span> = <span class="ty">IssuerCap</span> {
1088:             <span class="prop">id</span>: <span class="fn">object</span>::<span class="fn">new</span>(<span class="prop">ctx</span>),
1089:             <span class="prop">issuer_address</span>,
1090:             <span class="prop">issuer_name</span>: <span class="fn">string</span>::<span class="fn">utf8</span>(<span class="prop">issuer_name</span>),
1091:             <span class="prop">is_active</span>: <span class="kw">true</span>,
1092:         };
1093:         <span class="fn">transfer</span>::<span class="fn">transfer</span>(<span class="prop">cap</span>, <span class="prop">issuer_address</span>);
1094:     }
1095: }

1107: 
1108: <span class="cm"># 2. Build & verify</span>
1109: <span class="op">sui</span> move build --skip-fetch-latest-git-deps
1110: 
1111: <span class="cm"># 3. Test sebelum deploy</span>
1112: <span class="op">sui</span> move test
1113: 
1114: <span class="cm"># 4. Deploy ke Mainnet</span>
1115: <span class="op">sui</span> client publish \
1116:   --gas-budget <span class="num">100000000</span> \
1117:   --json
1118:

1120: <span class="cm"># "packageId": "0x..." ŌåÆ masuk ke .env</span>
