1127: <!-- ==================== SECTION 5: WALRUS ==================== -->
1128: <section class="section" id="walrus">
1129:   <div class="container">
1130:     <div class="section-label" data-num="05">WALRUS INTEGRATION</div>
1131:     <h2 class="section-title">Walrus Storage Layer</h2>
1132:     <p class="section-desc">Cara WalTrust menggunakan Walrus sebagai core storage ŌĆö bukan add-on. Ini adalah kunci untuk memenangkan bonus "Best Walrus Integration" senilai $200.</p>
1133: 
1134:     <div class="callout callout-green">
1135:       <span class="callout-icon">­¤Åå</span>
1136:       <div class="callout-text">
1137:         <strong>Winning formula Walrus:</strong> Simpan 2 blobs per credential ŌĆö (1) dokumen asli PDF/image, (2) metadata JSON. Blob ID keduanya di-store on-chain di SUI. Ini membuktikan <em>meaningful integration</em> yang juri cari.
1138:       </div>
1139:     </div>
1140: 
1141:     <h3>Walrus Endpoints</h3>
1142:     <div class="table-wrap">
1143:       <table>
1144:         <thead><tr><th>Endpoint</th><th>URL</th><th>Digunakan untuk</th></tr></thead>
1145:         <tbody>
1146:           <tr><td><strong>Publisher (Mainnet)</strong></td><td><code>https://publisher.walrus-mainnet.walrus.space</code></td><td>Upload dokumen credential</td></tr>
1147:           <tr><td><strong>Aggregator (Mainnet)</strong></td><td><code>https://aggregator.walrus-mainnet.walrus.space</code></td><td>Fetch dokumen untuk display</td></tr>
1148:           <tr><td><strong>Publisher (Testnet)</strong></td><td><code>https://publisher.walrus-testnet.walrus.space</code></td><td>Development & testing</td></tr>
1149:           <tr><td><strong>Aggregator (Testnet)</strong></td><td><code>https://aggregator.walrus-testnet.walrus.space</code></td><td>Development & testing</td></tr>
1150:         </tbody>
1151:       </table>
1152:     </div>
1153: 
1154:     <div class="code-wrap">
1155:       <div class="code-header">
1156:         <span class="code-file">app/lib/walrus.ts</span>
1157:         <span class="code-desc">Complete Walrus upload + fetch helper</span>
1158:       </div>
1159:       <div class="code-block">
1160: <span class="cm">// app/lib/walrus.ts</span>
1161: <span class="kw">const</span> <span class="prop">WALRUS_PUBLISHER</span> = <span class="str">"https://publisher.walrus-mainnet.walrus.space"</span>;
1162: <span class="kw">const</span> <span class="prop">WALRUS_AGGREGATOR</span> = <span class="str">"https://aggregator.walrus-mainnet.walrus.space"</span>;
1163: <span class="kw">const</span> <span class="prop">STORAGE_EPOCHS</span> = <span class="num">365</span>; <span class="cm">// ~1 tahun</span>
1164: 
1165: <span class="kw">export interface</span> <span class="ty">WalrusUploadResult</span> {
1166:   <span class="prop">blobId</span>: <span class="ty">string</span>;
1167:   <span class="prop">suiObjectId</span>: <span class="ty">string</span>;
1168:   <span class="prop">endEpoch</span>: <span class="ty">number</span>;
1169:   <span class="prop">isNewlyCreated</span>: <span class="ty">boolean</span>;
1170: }
1171: 
1172: <span class="kw">export interface</span> <span class="ty">CredentialMetadata</span> {
1173:   <span class="prop">title</span>: <span class="ty">string</span>;
1174:   <span class="prop">credentialType</span>: <span class="ty">string</span>;
1175:   <span class="prop">issuerName</span>: <span class="ty">string</span>;
1176:   <span class="prop">recipientName</span>: <span class="ty">string</span>;
1177:   <span class="prop">issuedAt</span>: <span class="ty">string</span>; <span class="cm">// ISO date</span>
1178:   <span class="prop">expiresAt</span>: <span class="ty">string</span> | <span class="kw">null</span>;
1179:   <span class="prop">additionalInfo</span>: <span class="ty">Record</span>&lt;<span class="ty">string</span>, <span class="ty">string</span>&gt;;
1180: }
1181: 
1182: <span class="cm">/**
1183:  * Upload file blob ke Walrus
1184:  * Returns blob ID yang akan disimpan on-chain di SUI
1185:  */</span>
1186: <span class="kw">export async function</span> <span class="fn">uploadToWalrus</span>(
1187:   <span class="prop">fileData</span>: <span class="ty">Uint8Array</span> | <span class="ty">Blob</span>,
1188:   <span class="prop">contentType</span>: <span class="ty">string</span> = <span class="str">"application/octet-stream"</span>
1189: ): <span class="ty">Promise</span>&lt;<span class="ty">WalrusUploadResult</span>&gt; {
1190:   <span class="kw">const</span> <span class="prop">response</span> = <span class="kw">await</span> <span class="fn">fetch</span>(
1191:     <span class="str">`</span><span class="prop">${WALRUS_PUBLISHER}</span><span class="str">/v1/blobs?epochs=</span><span class="prop">${STORAGE_EPOCHS}</span><span class="str">`</span>,
1192:     {
1193:       <span class="prop">method</span>: <span class="str">"PUT"</span>,
1194:       <span class="prop">headers</span>: { <span class="str">"Content-Type"</span>: <span class="prop">contentType</span> },
1195:       <span class="prop">body</span>: <span class="prop">fileData</span>,
1196:     }
1197:   );
1198: 
1199:   <span class="kw">if</span> (!<span class="prop">response</span>.<span class="prop">ok</span>) {
1200:     <span class="kw">throw new</span> <span class="fn">Error</span>(<span class="str">`Walrus upload failed: </span><span class="prop">${response.status}</span><span class="str">`</span>);
1201:   }
1202: 
1203:   <span class="kw">const</span> <span class="prop">result</span> = <span class="kw">await</span> <span class="prop">response</span>.<span class="fn">json</span>();
1204: 
1205:   <span class="cm">// Handle both newlyCreated and alreadyCertified responses</span>
1206:   <span class="kw">if</span> (<span class="prop">result</span>.<span class="prop">newlyCreated</span>) {
1207:     <span class="kw">return</span> {
1208:       <span class="prop">blobId</span>: <span class="prop">result</span>.<span class="prop">newlyCreated</span>.<span class="prop">blobObject</span>.<span class="prop">blobId</span>,
1209:       <span class="prop">suiObjectId</span>: <span class="prop">result</span>.<span class="prop">newlyCreated</span>.<span class="prop">blobObject</span>.<span class="prop">id</span>,
1210:       <span class="prop">endEpoch</span>: <span class="prop">result</span>.<span class="prop">newlyCreated</span>.<span class="prop">blobObject</span>.<span class="prop">storage</span>.<span class="prop">endEpoch</span>,
1211:       <span class="prop">isNewlyCreated</span>: <span class="kw">true</span>,
1212:     };
1213:   } <span class="kw">else if</span> (<span class="prop">result</span>.<span class="prop">alreadyCertified</span>) {
1214:     <span class="kw">return</span> {
1215:       <span class="prop">blobId</span>: <span class="prop">result</span>.<span class="prop">alreadyCertified</span>.<span class="prop">blobId</span>,
1216:       <span class="prop">suiObjectId</span>: <span class="str">""</span>,
1217:       <span class="prop">endEpoch</span>: <span class="prop">result</span>.<span class="prop">alreadyCertified</span>.<span class="prop">endEpoch</span>,
1218:       <span class="prop">isNewlyCreated</span>: <span class="kw">false</span>,
1219:     };
1220:   }
1221: 
1222:   <span class="kw">throw new</span> <span class="fn">Error</span>(<span class="str">"Unexpected Walrus response format"</span>);
1223: }

970:         <span class="prop">walrus_blob_id</span>: <span class="ty">vector</span>&lt;<span class="ty">u8</span>&gt;,
971:         <span class="prop">walrus_metadata_blob_id</span>: <span class="ty">vector</span>&lt;<span class="ty">u8</span>&gt;,
972:         <span class="prop">document_hash</span>: <span class="ty">vector</span>&lt;<span class="ty">u8</span>&gt;,
973:         <span class="prop">credential_type</span>: <span class="ty">vector</span>&lt;<span class="ty">u8</span>&gt;,
974:         <span class="prop">title</span>: <span class="ty">vector</span>&lt;<span class="ty">u8</span>&gt;,
975:         <span class="prop">recipient</span>: <span class="ty">address</span>,
976:         <span class="prop">recipient_name</span>: <span class="ty">vector</span>&lt;<span class="ty">u8</span>&gt;,
977:         <span class="prop">expires_at</span>: <span class="ty">u64</span>,
978:         <span class="prop">clock</span>: &<span class="ty">Clock</span>,
979:         <span class="prop">ctx</span>: &<span class="kw">mut</span> <span class="ty">TxContext</span>
980:     ) {
981:         <span class="fn">assert!</span>(<span class="prop">issuer_cap</span>.<span class="prop">is_active</span>, <span class="num">1001</span>); <span class="cm">// E_ISSUER_NOT_ACTIVE</span>
982: 
983:         <span class="kw">let</span> <span class="prop">issued_at</span> = <span class="fn">clock</span>::<span class="fn">timestamp_ms</span>(<span class="prop">clock</span>);
984:         <span class="kw">let</span> <span class="prop">credential_id</span> = <span class="fn">object</span>::<span class="fn">new</span>(<span class="prop">ctx</span>);
985:         <span class="kw">let</span> <span class="prop">cred_obj_id</span> = <span class="fn">object</span>::<span class="fn">uid_to_inner</span>(&<span class="prop">credential_id</span>);
986: 
987:         <span class="kw">let</span> <span class="prop">credential</span> = <span class="ty">Credential</span> {
988:             <span class="prop">id</span>: <span class="prop">credential_id</span>,
989:             <span class="prop">walrus_blob_id</span>: <span class="fn">string</span>::<span class="fn">utf8</span>(<span class="prop">walrus_blob_id</span>),
990:             <span class="prop">walrus_metadata_blob_id</span>: <span class="fn">string</span>::<span class="fn">utf8</span>(<span class="prop">walrus_metadata_blob_id</span>),
991:             <span class="prop">document_hash</span>,
992:             <span class="prop">credential_type</span>: <span class="fn">string</span>::<span class="fn">utf8</span>(<span class="prop">credential_type</span>),
993:             <span class="prop">title</span>: <span class="fn">string</span>::<span class="fn">utf8</span>(<span class="prop">title</span>),
994:             <span class="prop">issuer</span>: <span class="prop">issuer_cap</span>.<span class="prop">issuer_address</span>,
995:             <span class="prop">issuer_name</span>: <span class="prop">issuer_cap</span>.<span class="prop">issuer_name</span>,
996:             <span class="prop">recipient</span>,
997:             <span class="prop">recipient_name</span>: <span class="fn">string</span>::<span class="fn">utf8</span>(<span class="prop">recipient_name</span>),
998:             <span class="prop">issued_at</span>,
999:             <span class="prop">expires_at</span>,
1000:             <span class="prop">is_valid</span>: <span class="kw">true</span>,
1001:             <span class="prop">extra_fields</span>: <span class="fn">vec_map</span>::<span class="fn">empty</span>(),
1002:         };
1003: 
1004:         <span class="cm">// Emit event ŌĆö Tatum Data API bisa subscribe ke ini</span>
1005:         <span class="fn">event</span>::<span class="fn">emit</span>(<span class="ty">CredentialIssued</span> {
1006:             <span class="prop">credential_id</span>: <span class="prop">cred_obj_id</span>,
1007:             <span class="prop">issuer</span>: <span class="prop">issuer_cap</span>.<span class="prop">issuer_address</span>,
1008:             <span class="prop">recipient</span>,
1009:             <span class="prop">walrus_blob_id</span>: <span class="prop">credential</span>.<span class="prop">walrus_blob_id</span>,
1010:             <span class="prop">credential_type</span>: <span class="prop">credential</span>.<span class="prop">credential_type</span>,
1011:             <span class="prop">issued_at</span>,
1012:         });
1013: 
1014:         <span class="cm">// Transfer credential ke recipient</span>
1015:         <span class="fn">transfer</span>::<span class="fn">transfer</span>(<span class="prop">credential</span>, <span class="prop">recipient</span>);
1016:     }
1017: 
1018:     <span class="cm">/// Revoke credential ŌĆö hanya issuer asli yang bisa</span>
1019:     <span class="kw">public</span> <span class="kw">entry</span> <span class="kw">fun</span> <span class="fn">revoke_credential</span>(
1020:         <span class="prop">issuer_cap</span>: &<span class="ty">IssuerCap</span>,
1021:         <span class="prop">credential</span>: &<span class="kw">mut</span> <span class="ty">Credential</span>,
1022:         <span class="prop">clock</span>: &<span class="ty">Clock</span>,
1023:         <span class="prop">ctx</span>: &<span class="kw">mut</span> <span class="ty">TxContext</span>
1024:     ) {
1025:         <span class="fn">assert!</span>(<span class="prop">issuer_cap</span>.<span class="prop">issuer_address</span> == <span class="prop">credential</span>.<span class="prop">issuer</span>, <span class="num">1002</span>);
1026:         <span class="fn">assert!</span>(<span class="prop">credential</span>.<span class="prop">is_valid</span>, <span class="num">1003</span>); <span class="cm">// Already revoked</span>
1027: 
1028:         <span class="prop">credential</span>.<span class="prop">is_valid</span> = <span class="kw">false</span>;
1029: 
1030:         <span class="fn">event</span>::<span class="fn">emit</span>(<span class="ty">CredentialRevoked</span> {
1031:             <span class="prop">credential_id</span>: <span class="fn">object</span>::<span class="fn">uid_to_inner</span>(&<span class="prop">credential</span>.<span class="prop">id</span>),
1032:             <span class="prop">revoked_by</span>: <span class="fn">tx_context</span>::<span class="fn">sender</span>(<span class="prop">ctx</span>),
1033:             <span class="prop">revoked_at</span>: <span class="fn">clock</span>::<span class="fn">timestamp_ms</span>(<span class="prop">clock</span>),
1034:         });
1035:     }
1036: 
1037:     <span class="cm">/// Public verify ŌĆö siapa saja bisa query status credential</span>
1038:     <span class="kw">public</span> <span class="kw">fun</span> <span class="fn">verify_credential</span>(
1039:         <span class="prop">credential</span>: &<span class="ty">Credential</span>,
1040:         <span class="prop">clock</span>: &<span class="ty">Clock</span>,
1041:         <span class="prop">ctx</span>: &<span class="kw">mut</span> <span class="ty">TxContext</span>
1042:     ): <span class="ty">bool</span> {
1043:         <span class="kw">let</span> <span class="prop">now</span> = <span class="fn">clock</span>::<span class="fn">timestamp_ms</span>(<span class="prop">clock</span>);
1044:         <span class="kw">let</span> <span class="prop">not_expired</span> = <span class="prop">credential</span>.<span class="prop">expires_at</span> == <span class="num">0</span> || <span class="prop">now</span> &lt; <span class="prop">credential</span>.<span class="prop">expires_at</span>;
1045:         <span class="kw">let</span> <span class="prop">is_valid</span> = <span class="prop">credential</span>.<span class="prop">is_valid</span> &amp;&amp; <span class="prop">not_expired</span>;
1046: 
1047:         <span class="fn">event</span>::<span class="fn">emit</span>(<span class="ty">CredentialVerified</span> {
1048:             <span class="prop">credential_id</span>: <span class="fn">object</span>::<span class="fn">uid_to_inner</span>(&<span class="prop">credential</span>.<span class="prop">id</span>),
1049:             <span class="prop">verifier</span>: <span class="fn">tx_context</span>::<span class="fn">sender</span>(<span class="prop">ctx</span>),
1050:             <span class="prop">is_valid</span>,
1051:             <span class="prop">verified_at</span>: <span class="prop">now</span>,
1052:         });
1053:         <span class="prop">is_valid</span>
1054:     }
1055: 
1056:     <span class="cm">// ============ VIEW FUNCTIONS ============</span>
1057: 
1058:     <span class="kw">public</span> <span class="kw">fun</span> <span class="fn">get_walrus_blob_id</span>(<span class="prop">c</span>: &<span class="ty">Credential</span>): &<span class="ty">String</span> { &<span class="prop">c</span>.<span class="prop">walrus_blob_id</span> }
1059:     <span class="kw">public</span> <span class="kw">fun</span> <span class="fn">get_issuer</span>(<span class="prop">c</span>: &<span class="ty">Credential</span>): <span class="ty">address</span> { <span class="prop">c</span>.<span class="prop">issuer</span> }
1060:     <span class="kw">public</span> <span class="kw">fun</span> <span class="fn">get_recipient</span>(<span class="prop">c</span>: &<span class="ty">Credential</span>): <span class="ty">address</span> { <span class="prop">c</span>.<span class="prop">recipient</span> }
1061:     <span class="kw">public</span> <span class="kw">fun</span> <span class="fn">is_valid</span>(<span class="prop">c</span>: &<span class="ty">Credential</span>): <span class="ty">bool</span> { <span class="prop">c</span>.<span class="prop">is_valid</span> }
1062:     <span class="kw">public</span> <span class="kw">fun</span> <span class="fn">get_document_hash</span>(<span class="prop">c</span>: &<span class="ty">Credential</span>): &<span class="ty">vector</span>&lt;<span class="ty">u8</span>&gt; { &<span class="prop">c</span>.<span class="prop">document_hash</span> }
1063: }
1064:       </div>
1065:     </div>
1066: 
1067:     <div class="code-wrap">
1068:       <div class="code-header">
1069:         <span class="code-file">contracts/sources/issuer.move</span>
1070:         <span class="code-desc">Issuer registry ŌĆö admin approve issuer resmi</span>
1071:       </div>
1072:       <div class="code-block">
1073: <span class="kw">module</span> <span class="fn">waltrust</span>::<span class="fn">issuer</span> {
1074:     <span class="kw">use</span> <span class="fn">waltrust</span>::<span class="fn">credential</span>::{<span class="ty">AdminCap</span>, <span class="ty">IssuerCap</span>};
1075:     <span class="kw">use</span> <span class="fn">sui</span>::<span class="fn">object</span>::{<span class="ty">Self</span>, <span class="ty">UID</span>};
1076:     <span class="kw">use</span> <span class="fn">sui</span>::<span class="fn">transfer</span>;
1077:     <span class="kw">use</span> <span class="fn">sui</span>::<span class="fn">tx_context</span>::<span class="ty">TxContext</span>;
1078:     <span class="kw">use</span> <span class="fn">std</span>::<span class="fn">string</span>;
1079: 
1080:     <span class="cm">/// Admin approve issuer baru (universitas, lembaga sertifikasi)</span>
1081:     <span class="kw">public</span> <span class="kw">entry</span> <span class="kw">fun</span> <span class="fn">approve_issuer</span>(
1082:         <span class="prop">_admin</span>: &<span class="ty">AdminCap</span>,
1083:         <span class="prop">issuer_address</span>: <span class="ty">address</span>,
1084:         <span class="prop">issuer_name</span>: <span class="ty">vector</span>&lt;<span class="ty">u8</span>&gt;,
1085:         <span class="prop">ctx</span>: &<span class="kw">mut</span> <span class="ty">TxContext</span>
1086:     ) {
1087:         <span class="kw">let</span> <span class="prop">cap</span> = <span class="ty">IssuerCap</span> {
1088:             <span class="prop">id</span>: <span class="fn">object</span>::<span class="fn">new</span>(<span class="prop">ctx</span>),
1089:             <span class="prop">issuer_address</span>,
1090:             <span class="prop">issuer_name</span>: <span class="fn">string</span>::<span class="fn">utf8</span>(<span class="prop">issuer_name</span>),
1091:             <span class="prop">is_active</span>: <span class="kw">true</span>,
1092:         };
1093:         <span class="fn">transfer</span>::<span class="fn">transfer</span>(<span class="prop">cap</span>, <span class="prop">issuer_address</span>);
1094:     }
1095: }
1096:       </div>

1117:   --json

1126: 
1127: <!-- ==================== SECTION 5: WALRUS ==================== -->
1128: <section class="section" id="walrus">
1129:   <div class="container">
1130:     <div class="section-label" data-num="05">WALRUS INTEGRATION</div>
1131:     <h2 class="section-title">Walrus Storage Layer</h2>
1132:     <p class="section-desc">Cara WalTrust menggunakan Walrus sebagai core storage ŌĆö bukan add-on. Ini adalah kunci untuk memenangkan bonus "Best Walrus Integration" senilai $200.</p>
1133: 
1134:     <div class="callout callout-green">
1135:       <span class="callout-icon">­¤Åå</span>
1136:       <div class="callout-text">
1137:         <strong>Winning formula Walrus:</strong> Simpan 2 blobs per credential ŌĆö (1) dokumen asli PDF/image, (2) metadata JSON. Blob ID keduanya di-store on-chain di SUI. Ini membuktikan <em>meaningful integration</em> yang juri cari.
1138:       </div>
1139:     </div>
1140: 
1141:     <h3>Walrus Endpoints</h3>
1142:     <div class="table-wrap">
1143:       <table>
1144:         <thead><tr><th>Endpoint</th><th>URL</th><th>Digunakan untuk</th></tr></thead>
1145:         <tbody>
1146:           <tr><td><strong>Publisher (Mainnet)</strong></td><td><code>https://publisher.walrus-mainnet.walrus.space</code></td><td>Upload dokumen credential</td></tr>
1147:           <tr><td><strong>Aggregator (Mainnet)</strong></td><td><code>https://aggregator.walrus-mainnet.walrus.space</code></td><td>Fetch dokumen untuk display</td></tr>
1148:           <tr><td><strong>Publisher (Testnet)</strong></td><td><code>https://publisher.walrus-testnet.walrus.space</code></td><td>Development & testing</td></tr>
1149:           <tr><td><strong>Aggregator (Testnet)</strong></td><td><code>https://aggregator.walrus-testnet.walrus.space</code></td><td>Development & testing</td></tr>
1150:         </tbody>
1151:       </table>
1152:     </div>
1153: 
1154:     <div class="code-wrap">
1155:       <div class="code-header">
1156:         <span class="code-file">app/lib/walrus.ts</span>
1157:         <span class="code-desc">Complete Walrus upload + fetch helper</span>
1158:       </div>
1159:       <div class="code-block">
1160: <span class="cm">// app/lib/walrus.ts</span>
1161: <span class="kw">const</span> <span class="prop">WALRUS_PUBLISHER</span> = <span class="str">"https://publisher.walrus-mainnet.walrus.space"</span>;
1162: <span class="kw">const</span> <span class="prop">WALRUS_AGGREGATOR</span> = <span class="str">"https://aggregator.walrus-mainnet.walrus.space"</span>;
1163: <span class="kw">const</span> <span class="prop">STORAGE_EPOCHS</span> = <span class="num">365</span>; <span class="cm">// ~1 tahun</span>
1164: 
1165: <span class="kw">export interface</span> <span class="ty">WalrusUploadResult</span> {
1166:   <span class="prop">blobId</span>: <span class="ty">string</span>;
1167:   <span class="prop">suiObjectId</span>: <span class="ty">string</span>;
1168:   <span class="prop">endEpoch</span>: <span class="ty">number</span>;
1169:   <span class="prop">isNewlyCreated</span>: <span class="ty">boolean</span>;
1170: }
1171: 
1172: <span class="kw">export interface</span> <span class="ty">CredentialMetadata</span> {
1173:   <span class="prop">title</span>: <span class="ty">string</span>;
1174:   <span class="prop">credentialType</span>: <span class="ty">string</span>;
1175:   <span class="prop">issuerName</span>: <span class="ty">string</span>;
1176:   <span class="prop">recipientName</span>: <span class="ty">string</span>;
1177:   <span class="prop">issuedAt</span>: <span class="ty">string</span>; <span class="cm">// ISO date</span>
1178:   <span class="prop">expiresAt</span>: <span class="ty">string</span> | <span class="kw">null</span>;
1179:   <span class="prop">additionalInfo</span>: <span class="ty">Record</span>&lt;<span class="ty">string</span>, <span class="ty">string</span>&gt;;
1180: }
1181: 
1182: <span class="cm">/**
1183:  * Upload file blob ke Walrus
1184:  * Returns blob ID yang akan disimpan on-chain di SUI
1185:  */</span>
1186: <span class="kw">export async function</span> <span class="fn">uploadToWalrus</span>(
1187:   <span class="prop">fileData</span>: <span class="ty">Uint8Array</span> | <span class="ty">Blob</span>,
1188:   <span class="prop">contentType</span>: <span class="ty">string</span> = <span class="str">"application/octet-stream"</span>
1189: ): <span class="ty">Promise</span>&lt;<span class="ty">WalrusUploadResult</span>&gt; {
1190:   <span class="kw">const</span> <span class="prop">response</span> = <span class="kw">await</span> <span class="fn">fetch</span>(
1191:     <span class="str">`</span><span class="prop">${WALRUS_PUBLISHER}</span><span class="str">/v1/blobs?epochs=</span><span class="prop">${STORAGE_EPOCHS}</span><span class="str">`</span>,
1192:     {
1193:       <span class="prop">method</span>: <span class="str">"PUT"</span>,
1194:       <span class="prop">headers</span>: { <span class="str">"Content-Type"</span>: <span class="prop">contentType</span> },
1195:       <span class="prop">body</span>: <span class="prop">fileData</span>,
1196:     }
1197:   );
1198: 
1199:   <span class="kw">if</span> (!<span class="prop">response</span>.<span class="prop">ok</span>) {
1200:     <span class="kw">throw new</span> <span class="fn">Error</span>(<span class="str">`Walrus upload failed: </span><span class="prop">${response.status}</span><span class="str">`</span>);
1201:   }
1202: 
1203:   <span class="kw">const</span> <span class="prop">result</span> = <span class="kw">await</span> <span class="prop">response</span>.<span class="fn">json</span>();
1204: 
1205:   <span class="cm">// Handle both newlyCreated and alreadyCertified responses</span>
1206:   <span class="kw">if</span> (<span class="prop">result</span>.<span class="prop">newlyCreated</span>) {
1207:     <span class="kw">return</span> {
1208:       <span class="prop">blobId</span>: <span class="prop">result</span>.<span class="prop">newlyCreated</span>.<span class="prop">blobObject</span>.<span class="prop">blobId</span>,
1209:       <span class="prop">suiObjectId</span>: <span class="prop">result</span>.<span class="prop">newlyCreated</span>.<span class="prop">blobObject</span>.<span class="prop">id</span>,
1210:       <span class="prop">endEpoch</span>: <span class="prop">result</span>.<span class="prop">newlyCreated</span>.<span class="prop">blobObject</span>.<span class="prop">storage</span>.<span class="prop">endEpoch</span>,
1211:       <span class="prop">isNewlyCreated</span>: <span class="kw">true</span>,
1212:     };
1213:   } <span class="kw">else if</span> (<span class="prop">result</span>.<span class="prop">alreadyCertified</span>) {
1214:     <span class="kw">return</span> {
1215:       <span class="prop">blobId</span>: <span class="prop">result</span>.<span class="prop">alreadyCertified</span>.<span class="prop">blobId</span>,
1216:       <span class="prop">suiObjectId</span>: <span class="str">""</span>,
1217:       <span class="prop">endEpoch</span>: <span class="prop">result</span>.<span class="prop">alreadyCertified</span>.<span class="prop">endEpoch</span>,
1218:       <span class="prop">isNewlyCreated</span>: <span class="kw">false</span>,
1219:     };
1220:   }
1221: 
1222:   <span class="kw">throw new</span> <span class="fn">Error</span>(<span class="str">"Unexpected Walrus response format"</span>);
1223: }
1224: 
1225: <span class="cm">/**
1226:  * Upload metadata JSON ke Walrus
1227:  * Metadata berisi info credential yang bisa dibaca tanpa buka PDF
1228:  */</span>
1229: <span class="kw">export async function</span> <span class="fn">uploadMetadataToWalrus</span>(
1230:   <span class="prop">metadata</span>: <span class="ty">CredentialMetadata</span>
1231: ): <span class="ty">Promise</span>&lt;<span class="ty">WalrusUploadResult</span>&gt; {
1232:   <span class="kw">const</span> <span class="prop">jsonBytes</span> = <span class="kw">new</span> <span class="fn">TextEncoder</span>().<span class="fn">encode</span>(<span class="fn">JSON</span>.<span class="fn">stringify</span>(<span class="prop">metadata</span>));
1233:   <span class="kw">return</span> <span class="fn">uploadToWalrus</span>(<span class="prop">jsonBytes</span>, <span class="str">"application/json"</span>);
1234: }
1235: 
1236: <span class="cm">/**
1237:  * Fetch blob dari Walrus by Blob ID
1238:  * Digunakan di verifier page untuk tampilkan dokumen
1239:  */</span>
1240: <span class="kw">export async function</span> <span class="fn">fetchFromWalrus</span>(<span class="prop">blobId</span>: <span class="ty">string</span>): <span class="ty">Promise</span>&lt;<span class="ty">Blob</span>&gt; {
1241:   <span class="kw">const</span> <span class="prop">response</span> = <span class="kw">await</span> <span class="fn">fetch</span>(
1242:     <span class="str">`</span><span class="prop">${WALRUS_AGGREGATOR}</span><span class="str">/v1/blobs/</span><span class="prop">${blobId}</span><span class="str">`</span>
1243:   );
1244: 
1245:   <span class="kw">if</span> (!<span class="prop">response</span>.<span class="prop">ok</span>) {
1246:     <span class="kw">throw new</span> <span class="fn">Error</span>(<span class="str">`Walrus fetch failed for blob: </span><span class="prop">${blobId}</span><span class="str">`</span>);
1247:   }
1248: 
1249:   <span class="kw">return</span> <span class="prop">response</span>.<span class="fn">blob</span>();
1250: }
1251: 
1252: <span class="cm">/**
1253:  * Fetch metadata JSON dari Walrus
1254:  */</span>
1255: <span class="kw">export async function</span> <span class="fn">fetchMetadataFromWalrus</span>(
1256:   <span class="prop">metadataBlobId</span>: <span class="ty">string</span>
1257: ): <span class="ty">Promise</span>&lt;<span class="ty">CredentialMetadata</span>&gt; {
1258:   <span class="kw">const</span> <span class="prop">blob</span> = <span class="kw">await</span> <span class="fn">fetchFromWalrus</span>(<span class="prop">metadataBlobId</span>);
1259:   <span class="kw">const</span> <span class="prop">text</span> = <span class="kw">await</span> <span class="prop">blob</span>.<span class="fn">text</span>();
1260:   <span class="kw">return</span> <span class="fn">JSON</span>.<span class="fn">parse</span>(<span class="prop">text</span>) <span class="kw">as</span> <span class="ty">CredentialMetadata</span>;
1261: }
1262: 
1263: <span class="cm">/**
1264:  * Compute SHA-256 hash dari file (untuk on-chain verification)
1265:  */</span>
1266: <span class="kw">export async function</span> <span class="fn">hashFile</span>(<span class="prop">fileData</span>: <span class="ty">ArrayBuffer</span>): <span class="ty">Promise</span>&lt;<span class="ty">Uint8Array</span>&gt; {
1267:   <span class="kw">const</span> <span class="prop">hashBuffer</span> = <span class="kw">await</span> <span class="prop">crypto</span>.<span class="prop">subtle</span>.<span class="fn">digest</span>(<span class="str">"SHA-256"</span>, <span class="prop">fileData</span>);
1268:   <span class="kw">return new</span> <span class="fn">Uint8Array</span>(<span class="prop">hashBuffer</span>);
1269: }
1270:       </div>
1271:     </div>
1272:   </div>
1273: </section>

1275: <!-- ==================== SECTION 6: TATUM ==================== -->
1276: <section class="section" id="tatum">
1277:   <div class="container">
1278:     <div class="section-label" data-num="06">TATUM RPC INTEGRATION</div>
1279:     <h2 class="section-title">Tatum RPC ŌĆö SuiClient Configuration</h2>
1280:     <p class="section-desc">Semua on-chain call wajib melalui Tatum endpoint. Ini adalah requirement utama yang tidak boleh dilupakan.</p>
1281: 
1282:     <div class="callout callout-amber">
1283:       <span class="callout-icon">ŌÜĀ’ĖÅ</span>
1284:       <div class="callout-text">
1285:         <strong>WAJIB:</strong> Jangan pernah pakai public SUI RPC (<code>https://fullnode.mainnet.sui.io</code>) di kode yang di-submit. Semua query harus via Tatum. Juri akan cek kode dan README.
1286:       </div>
1287:     </div>
1288: 
1289:     <div class="code-wrap">
1290:       <div class="code-header">
1291:         <span class="code-file">app/lib/sui-client.ts</span>

1293:       </div>
1294:       <div class="code-block">
1295: <span class="cm">// app/lib/sui-client.ts</span>
1296: <span class="kw">import</span> { <span class="ty">SuiClient</span>, <span class="ty">getFullnodeUrl</span> } <span class="kw">from</span> <span class="str">"@mysten/sui/client"</span>;
1297: 
1298: <span class="kw">const</span> <span class="prop">TATUM_API_KEY</span> = <span class="prop">process</span>.<span class="prop">env</span>.<span class="prop">TATUM_API_KEY</span>!;
1299: 
1300: <span class="cm">// Tatum RPC endpoints untuk SUI</span>
1301: <span class="kw">export const</span> <span class="prop">TATUM_ENDPOINTS</span> = {
1302:   <span class="prop">mainnet</span>: <span class="str">"https://sui-mainnet.gateway.tatum.io"</span>,
1303:   <span class="prop">testnet</span>: <span class="str">"https://sui-testnet.gateway.tatum.io"</span>,
1304:   <span class="prop">devnet</span>:  <span class="str">"https://sui-devnet.gateway.tatum.io"</span>,
1305: };
1306: 
1307: <span class="cm">/**
1308:  * Singleton SuiClient via Tatum RPC
1309:  * Gunakan ini di SELURUH aplikasi ŌĆö jangan buat SuiClient baru
1310:  */</span>
1311: <span class="kw">export function</span> <span class="fn">createTatumSuiClient</span>(
1312:   <span class="prop">network</span>: <span class="str">"mainnet"</span> | <span class="str">"testnet"</span> | <span class="str">"devnet"</span> = <span class="str">"mainnet"</span>
1313: ): <span class="ty">SuiClient</span> {
1314:   <span class="kw">return new</span> <span class="fn">SuiClient</span>({
1315:     <span class="prop">url</span>: <span class="prop">TATUM_ENDPOINTS</span>[<span class="prop">network</span>],
1316:     <span class="cm">// Inject Tatum API key ke setiap request</span>
1317:     <span class="prop">rpcClient</span>: {
1318:       <span class="prop">requestMiddleware</span>: (<span class="prop">params</span>) => ({
1319:         ...<span class="prop">params</span>,
1320:         <span class="prop">headers</span>: {
1321:           ...<span class="prop">params</span>.<span class="prop">headers</span>,
1322:           <span class="str">"x-api-key"</span>: <span class="prop">TATUM_API_KEY</span>,
1323:         },
1324:       }),
1325:     },
1326:   });
1327: }
1328: 
1329: <span class="cm">// Singleton instances</span>
1330: <span class="kw">export const</span> <span class="prop">suiClient</span> = <span class="fn">createTatumSuiClient</span>(<span class="str">"mainnet"</span>);
1331: 
1332: <span class="cm">// Package address setelah deploy</span>
1333: <span class="kw">export const</span> <span class="prop">CONTRACT</span> = {
1334:   <span class="prop">packageId</span>: <span class="prop">process</span>.<span class="prop">env</span>.<span class="prop">NEXT_PUBLIC_PACKAGE_ID</span>!,
1335:   <span class="prop">credentialModule</span>: <span class="str">"credential"</span>,
1336:   <span class="prop">issuerModule</span>: <span class="str">"issuer"</span>,
1337: };
1338:       </div>
1339:     </div>

1346:       <div class="code-block">
1347: <span class="cm">// app/lib/contract.ts</span>
1348: <span class="kw">import</span> { <span class="ty">Transaction</span> } <span class="kw">from</span> <span class="str">"@mysten/sui/transactions"</span>;
1349: <span class="kw">import</span> { <span class="prop">suiClient</span>, <span class="prop">CONTRACT</span> } <span class="kw">from</span> <span class="str">"./sui-client"</span>;
1350: <span class="kw">import</span> <span class="kw">type</span> { <span class="ty">SignAndExecuteTransaction</span> } <span class="kw">from</span> <span class="str">"@mysten/dapp-kit"</span>;
1351: 
1352: <span class="cm">/**
1353:  * Issue credential on-chain
1354:  * Dipanggil setelah Walrus upload selesai
1355:  */</span>
1356: <span class="kw">export async function</span> <span class="fn">issueCredentialTx</span>(
1357:   <span class="prop">params</span>: {
1358:     <span class="prop">issuerCapId</span>: <span class="ty">string</span>;
1359:     <span class="prop">walrusBlobId</span>: <span class="ty">string</span>;
1360:     <span class="prop">walrusMetadataBlobId</span>: <span class="ty">string</span>;
1361:     <span class="prop">documentHash</span>: <span class="ty">Uint8Array</span>;
1362:     <span class="prop">credentialType</span>: <span class="ty">string</span>;
1363:     <span class="prop">title</span>: <span class="ty">string</span>;
1364:     <span class="prop">recipient</span>: <span class="ty">string</span>;
1365:     <span class="prop">recipientName</span>: <span class="ty">string</span>;
1366:     <span class="prop">expiresAt</span>: <span class="ty">number</span>; <span class="cm">// 0 = no expiry</span>
1367:   },
1368:   <span class="prop">signAndExecute</span>: <span class="ty">SignAndExecuteTransaction</span>
1369: ) {
1370:   <span class="kw">const</span> <span class="prop">tx</span> = <span class="kw">new</span> <span class="fn">Transaction</span>();
1371: 
1372:   <span class="prop">tx</span>.<span class="fn">moveCall</span>({
1373:     <span class="prop">target</span>: <span class="str">`</span><span class="prop">${CONTRACT.packageId}</span><span class="str">::</span><span class="prop">${CONTRACT.credentialModule}</span><span class="str">::issue_credential`</span>,
1374:     <span class="prop">arguments</span>: [
1375:       <span class="prop">tx</span>.<span class="fn">object</span>(<span class="prop">params</span>.<span class="prop">issuerCapId</span>),
1376:       <span class="prop">tx</span>.<span class="fn">pure</span>.<span class="fn">vector</span>(<span class="str">"u8"</span>, <span class="kw">new</span> <span class="fn">TextEncoder</span>().<span class="fn">encode</span>(<span class="prop">params</span>.<span class="prop">walrusBlobId</span>)),
1377:       <span class="prop">tx</span>.<span class="fn">pure</span>.<span class="fn">vector</span>(<span class="str">"u8"</span>, <span class="kw">new</span> <span class="fn">TextEncoder</span>().<span class="fn">encode</span>(<span class="prop">params</span>.<span class="prop">walrusMetadataBlobId</span>)),
1378:       <span class="prop">tx</span>.<span class="fn">pure</span>.<span class="fn">vector</span>(<span class="str">"u8"</span>, <span class="prop">params</span>.<span class="prop">documentHash</span>),
1379:       <span class="prop">tx</span>.<span class="fn">pure</span>.<span class="fn">vector</span>(<span class="str">"u8"</span>, <span class="kw">new</span> <span class="fn">TextEncoder</span>().<span class="fn">encode</span>(<span class="prop">params</span>.<span class="prop">credentialType</span>)),
1380:       <span class="prop">tx</span>.<span class="fn">pure</span>.<span class="fn">vector</span>(<span class="str">"u8"</span>, <span class="kw">new</span> <span class="fn">TextEncoder</span>().<span class="fn">encode</span>(<span class="prop">params</span>.<span class="prop">title</span>)),
1381:       <span class="prop">tx</span>.<span class="fn">pure</span>.<span class="fn">address</span>(<span class="prop">params</span>.<span class="prop">recipient</span>),
1382:       <span class="prop">tx</span>.<span class="fn">pure</span>.<span class="fn">vector</span>(<span class="str">"u8"</span>, <span class="kw">new</span> <span class="fn">TextEncoder</span>().<span class="fn">encode</span>(<span class="prop">params</span>.<span class="prop">recipientName</span>)),
1383:       <span class="prop">tx</span>.<span class="fn">pure</span>.<span class="fn">u64</span>(<span class="prop">params</span>.<span class="prop">expiresAt</span>),
1384:       <span class="prop">tx</span>.<span class="fn">object</span>(<span class="str">"0x6"</span>), <span class="cm">// Sui Clock object (always 0x6)</span>
1385:     ],
1386:   });
1387: 
1388:   <span class="kw">return</span> <span class="fn">signAndExecute</span>({ <span class="prop">transaction</span>: <span class="prop">tx</span> });
1389: }
1390: 
1391: <span class="cm">/**
1392:  * Query credential object dari SUI via Tatum RPC
1393:  */</span>
1394: <span class="kw">export async function</span> <span class="fn">getCredential</span>(<span class="prop">credentialObjectId</span>: <span class="ty">string</span>) {
1395:   <span class="kw">return</span> <span class="prop">suiClient</span>.<span class="fn">getObject</span>({
1396:     <span class="prop">id</span>: <span class="prop">credentialObjectId</span>,
1397:     <span class="prop">options</span>: {
1398:       <span class="prop">showContent</span>: <span class="kw">true</span>,
1399:       <span class="prop">showOwner</span>: <span class="kw">true</span>,
1400:       <span class="prop">showType</span>: <span class="kw">true</span>,
1401:     },
1402:   });
1403: }
1404: 
1405: <span class="cm">/**
1406:  * Get semua credential milik wallet address tertentu
1407:  */</span>
1408: <span class="kw">export async function</span> <span class="fn">getWalletCredentials</span>(<span class="prop">walletAddress</span>: <span class="ty">string</span>) {
1409:   <span class="kw">const</span> <span class="prop">objects</span> = <span class="kw">await</span> <span class="prop">suiClient</span>.<span class="fn">getOwnedObjects</span>({
1410:     <span class="prop">owner</span>: <span class="prop">walletAddress</span>,
1411:     <span class="prop">filter</span>: {
1412:       <span class="prop">StructType</span>: <span class="str">`</span><span class="prop">${CONTRACT.packageId}</span><span class="str">::credential::Credential`</span>,
1413:     },
1414:     <span class="prop">options</span>: { <span class="prop">showContent</span>: <span class="kw">true</span>, <span class="prop">showType</span>: <span class="kw">true</span> },
1415:   });
1416:   <span class="kw">return</span> <span class="prop">objects</span>.<span class="prop">data</span>;
1417: }
1418:       </div>
1419:     </div>

1423: <!-- ==================== SECTION 7: FRONTEND ==================== -->
1424: <section class="section" id="frontend">
1425:   <div class="container">
1426:     <div class="section-label" data-num="07">FRONTEND PAGES</div>
1427:     <h2 class="section-title">Frontend ŌĆö 3 Core Pages</h2>
1428:     <p class="section-desc">Tiga halaman utama yang harus dibangun. Prioritaskan Verifier Page karena ini yang paling sering di-demo ke juri.</p>
1429: 
1430:     <div class="grid-3" style="margin-bottom: 2rem;">
1431:       <div class="card card-green">
1432:         <div class="arch-label" style="text-align:left; color: var(--green); font-size: 10px; margin-bottom: 6px;">PRIORITY 1</div>
1433:         <div style="font-weight: 600; font-size: 15px; margin-bottom: 6px;">Verifier Page</div>
1434:         <p style="font-size: 13px;">Input credential ID / wallet address ŌåÆ instant verification result + preview dokumen dari Walrus. Zero login needed.</p>
1435:         <code style="font-size: 11px;">/verify/[credentialId]</code>
1436:       </div>
1437:       <div class="card card-blue">
1438:         <div class="arch-label" style="text-align:left; color: var(--blue); font-size: 10px; margin-bottom: 6px;">PRIORITY 2</div>
1439:         <div style="font-weight: 600; font-size: 15px; margin-bottom: 6px;">Issuer Dashboard</div>
1440:         <p style="font-size: 13px;">Connect wallet ŌåÆ upload dokumen ke Walrus ŌåÆ fill form ŌåÆ issue credential on-chain via Tatum RPC.</p>
1441:         <code style="font-size: 11px;">/issue</code>
1442:       </div>
1443:       <div class="card">
1444:         <div class="arch-label" style="text-align:left; color: var(--amber); font-size: 10px; margin-bottom: 6px;">PRIORITY 3</div>
1445:         <div style="font-weight: 600; font-size: 15px; margin-bottom: 6px;">Holder Wallet</div>
1446:         <p style="font-size: 13px;">Connect wallet ŌåÆ lihat semua credential ŌåÆ copy share link ŌåÆ share ke employer.</p>
1447:         <code style="font-size: 11px;">/wallet</code>
1448:       </div>
1449:     </div>
1450: 
1451:     <div class="code-wrap">
1452:       <div class="code-header">
1453:         <span class="code-file">app/app/verify/[id]/page.tsx</span>
1454:         <span class="code-desc">Verifier page ŌĆö paling penting untuk demo</span>
1455:       </div>
1456:       <div class="code-block">
1457: <span class="str">"use client"</span>;
1458: <span class="kw">import</span> { <span class="ty">useEffect</span>, <span class="ty">useState</span> } <span class="kw">from</span> <span class="str">"react"</span>;
1459: <span class="kw">import</span> { <span class="fn">getCredential</span> } <span class="kw">from</span> <span class="str">"@/lib/contract"</span>;
1460: <span class="kw">import</span> { <span class="fn">fetchMetadataFromWalrus</span>, <span class="fn">fetchFromWalrus</span> } <span class="kw">from</span> <span class="str">"@/lib/walrus"</span>;
1461: 
1462: <span class="kw">type</span> <span class="ty">VerifyStatus</span> = <span class="str">"loading"</span> | <span class="str">"valid"</span> | <span class="str">"revoked"</span> | <span class="str">"expired"</span> | <span class="str">"not_found"</span>;
1463: 
1464: <span class="kw">export default function</span> <span class="fn">VerifyPage</span>({ <span class="prop">params</span> }: { <span class="prop">params</span>: { <span class="prop">id</span>: <span class="ty">string</span> } }) {
1465:   <span class="kw">const</span> [<span class="prop">status</span>, <span class="fn">setStatus</span>] = <span class="fn">useState</span>&lt;<span class="ty">VerifyStatus</span>&gt;(<span class="str">"loading"</span>);
1466:   <span class="kw">const</span> [<span class="prop">credential</span>, <span class="fn">setCredential</span>] = <span class="fn">useState</span>&lt;<span class="kw">any</span>&gt;(<span class="kw">null</span>);
1467:   <span class="kw">const</span> [<span class="prop">metadata</span>, <span class="fn">setMetadata</span>] = <span class="fn">useState</span>&lt;<span class="kw">any</span>&gt;(<span class="kw">null</span>);
1468:   <span class="kw">const</span> [<span class="prop">docUrl</span>, <span class="fn">setDocUrl</span>] = <span class="fn">useState</span>&lt;<span class="ty">string</span> | <span class="kw">null</span>&gt;(<span class="kw">null</span>);
1469: 
1470:   <span class="fn">useEffect</span>(<span class="kw">async</span> () => {
1471:     <span class="kw">try</span> {
1472:       <span class="cm">// 1. Query credential on-chain via Tatum RPC</span>
1473:       <span class="kw">const</span> <span class="prop">obj</span> = <span class="kw">await</span> <span class="fn">getCredential</span>(<span class="prop">params</span>.<span class="prop">id</span>);
1474:       <span class="kw">if</span> (!<span class="prop">obj</span>.<span class="prop">data</span>) { <span class="fn">setStatus</span>(<span class="str">"not_found"</span>); <span class="kw">return</span>; }
1475: 
1476:       <span class="kw">const</span> <span class="prop">fields</span> = (<span class="prop">obj</span>.<span class="prop">data</span>.<span class="prop">content</span> <span class="kw">as</span> <span class="kw">any</span>).<span class="prop">fields</span>;
1477:       <span class="fn">setCredential</span>(<span class="prop">fields</span>);
1478: 
1479:       <span class="cm">// 2. Check validity</span>
1480:       <span class="kw">if</span> (!<span class="prop">fields</span>.<span class="prop">is_valid</span>) { <span class="fn">setStatus</span>(<span class="str">"revoked"</span>); <span class="kw">return</span>; }
1481:       <span class="kw">const</span> <span class="prop">now</span> = <span class="fn">Date</span>.<span class="fn">now</span>();
1482:       <span class="kw">if</span> (<span class="prop">fields</span>.<span class="prop">expires_at</span> > <span class="num">0</span> && <span class="prop">now</span> > <span class="fn">Number</span>(<span class="prop">fields</span>.<span class="prop">expires_at</span>)) {
1483:         <span class="fn">setStatus</span>(<span class="str">"expired"</span>); <span class="kw">return</span>;
1484:       }
1485: 
1486:       <span class="cm">// 3. Fetch metadata dari Walrus</span>
1487:       <span class="kw">const</span> <span class="prop">meta</span> = <span class="kw">await</span> <span class="fn">fetchMetadataFromWalrus</span>(<span class="prop">fields</span>.<span class="prop">walrus_metadata_blob_id</span>);
1488:       <span class="fn">setMetadata</span>(<span class="prop">meta</span>);
1489: 
1490:       <span class="cm">// 4. Fetch dokumen asli dari Walrus (PDF/image)</span>
1491:       <span class="kw">const</span> <span class="prop">docBlob</span> = <span class="kw">await</span> <span class="fn">fetchFromWalrus</span>(<span class="prop">fields</span>.<span class="prop">walrus_blob_id</span>);
1492:       <span class="fn">setDocUrl</span>(<span class="fn">URL</span>.<span class="fn">createObjectURL</span>(<span class="prop">docBlob</span>));
1493:       <span class="fn">setStatus</span>(<span class="str">"valid"</span>);
1494:     } <span class="kw">catch</span> {
1495:       <span class="fn">setStatus</span>(<span class="str">"not_found"</span>);
1496:     }
1497:   }, [<span class="prop">params</span>.<span class="prop">id</span>]);
1498: 
1499:   <span class="kw">return</span> (
1500:     &lt;<span class="fn">div</span> <span class="prop">className</span>=<span class="str">"max-w-2xl mx-auto p-6"</span>&gt;
1501:       {<span class="prop">status</span> === <span class="str">"loading"</span> && &lt;<span class="fn">VerifyLoading</span> /&gt;}
1502:       {<span class="prop">status</span> === <span class="str">"valid"</span> && &lt;<span class="fn">VerifySuccess</span> <span class="prop">credential</span>={<span class="prop">credential</span>} <span class="prop">metadata</span>={<span class="prop">metadata</span>} <span class="prop">docUrl</span>={<span class="prop">docUrl</span>} /&gt;}
1503:       {<span class="prop">status</span> === <span class="str">"revoked"</span> && &lt;<span class="fn">VerifyRevoked</span> <span class="prop">credential</span>={<span class="prop">credential</span>} /&gt;}
1504:       {<span class="prop">status</span> === <span class="str">"expired"</span> && &lt;<span class="fn">VerifyExpired</span> <span class="prop">credential</span>={<span class="prop">credential</span>} /&gt;}
1505:       {<span class="prop">status</span> === <span class="str">"not_found"</span> && &lt;<span class="fn">VerifyNotFound</span> /&gt;}
1506:     &lt;/<span class="fn">div</span>&gt;
1507:   );
1508: }
1509:       </div>
1510:     </div>
1511: 
1512:     <div class="code-wrap">
1513:       <div class="code-header">
1514:         <span class="code-file">app/.env.local</span>
1515:         <span class="code-desc">Environment variables yang diperlukan</span>
1516:       </div>
1517:       <div class="code-block">
1518: <span class="cm"># Tatum API Key ŌĆö dari dashboard.tatum.io</span>
1519: <span class="prop">TATUM_API_KEY</span>=<span class="str">your_tatum_api_key_here</span>
1520: 
1521: <span class="cm"># SUI Smart Contract (setelah deploy)</span>
1522: <span class="prop">NEXT_PUBLIC_PACKAGE_ID</span>=<span class="str">0x...</span>
1523: <span class="prop">NEXT_PUBLIC_NETWORK</span>=<span class="str">mainnet</span>

1550: <span class="kw">export async function</span> <span class="fn">POST</span>(<span class="prop">req</span>: <span class="ty">NextRequest</span>) {
1551:   <span class="kw">try</span> {

1553:     <span class="kw">const</span> <span class="prop">file</span> = <span class="prop">formData</span>.<span class="fn">get</span>(<span class="str">"document"</span>) <span class="kw">as</span> <span class="ty">File</span>;
1554:     <span class="kw">const</span> <span class="prop">metadataStr</span> = <span class="prop">formData</span>.<span class="fn">get</span>(<span class="str">"metadata"</span>) <span class="kw">as</span> <span class="ty">string</span>;
1555: 
1556:     <span class="kw">if</span> (!<span class="prop">file</span>) {
1557:       <span class="kw">return</span> <span class="ty">NextResponse</span>.<span class="fn">json</span>({ <span class="prop">error</span>: <span class="str">"No file"</span> }, { <span class="prop">status</span>: <span class="num">400</span> });
1558:     }
1559: 
1560:     <span class="cm">// Validasi file type</span>
1561:     <span class="kw">const</span> <span class="prop">allowedTypes</span> = [<span class="str">"application/pdf"</span>, <span class="str">"image/jpeg"</span>, <span class="str">"image/png"</span>];

1563:       <span class="kw">return</span> <span class="ty">NextResponse</span>.<span class="fn">json</span>({ <span class="prop">error</span>: <span class="str">"Invalid file type"</span> }, { <span class="prop">status</span>: <span class="num">400</span> });
1564:     }
1565: 
1566:     <span class="cm">// Max 10MB</span>
1567:     <span class="kw">if</span> (<span class="prop">file</span>.<span class="prop">size</span> > <span class="num">10</span> * <span class="num">1024</span> * <span class="num">1024</span>) {

1569:     }

1307: <span class="cm">/**
1308:  * Singleton SuiClient via Tatum RPC
1309:  * Gunakan ini di SELURUH aplikasi ŌĆö jangan buat SuiClient baru
1310:  */</span>
1311: <span class="kw">export function</span> <span class="fn">createTatumSuiClient</span>(
1312:   <span class="prop">network</span>: <span class="str">"mainnet"</span> | <span class="str">"testnet"</span> | <span class="str">"devnet"</span> = <span class="str">"mainnet"</span>
1313: ): <span class="ty">SuiClient</span> {
1314:   <span class="kw">return new</span> <span class="fn">SuiClient</span>({
1315:     <span class="prop">url</span>: <span class="prop">TATUM_ENDPOINTS</span>[<span class="prop">network</span>],
1316:     <span class="cm">// Inject Tatum API key ke setiap request</span>
1317:     <span class="prop">rpcClient</span>: {
1318:       <span class="prop">requestMiddleware</span>: (<span class="prop">params</span>) => ({
1319:         ...<span class="prop">params</span>,
1320:         <span class="prop">headers</span>: {
1321:           ...<span class="prop">params</span>.<span class="prop">headers</span>,
1322:           <span class="str">"x-api-key"</span>: <span class="prop">TATUM_API_KEY</span>,
1323:         },
1324:       }),
1325:     },
1326:   });
1327: }
1328: 
1329: <span class="cm">// Singleton instances</span>
1330: <span class="kw">export const</span> <span class="prop">suiClient</span> = <span class="fn">createTatumSuiClient</span>(<span class="str">"mainnet"</span>);
1331: 
1332: <span class="cm">// Package address setelah deploy</span>
1333: <span class="kw">export const</span> <span class="prop">CONTRACT</span> = {
1334:   <span class="prop">packageId</span>: <span class="prop">process</span>.<span class="prop">env</span>.<span class="prop">NEXT_PUBLIC_PACKAGE_ID</span>!,
1335:   <span class="prop">credentialModule</span>: <span class="str">"credential"</span>,
1336:   <span class="prop">issuerModule</span>: <span class="str">"issuer"</span>,
1337: };
1338:       </div>
1339:     </div>
1340: 
1341:     <div class="code-wrap">
1342:       <div class="code-header">
1343:         <span class="code-file">app/lib/contract.ts</span>
1344:         <span class="code-desc">Helper functions untuk semua Move calls via Tatum</span>
1345:       </div>
1346:       <div class="code-block">
1347: <span class="cm">// app/lib/contract.ts</span>
1348: <span class="kw">import</span> { <span class="ty">Transaction</span> } <span class="kw">from</span> <span class="str">"@mysten/sui/transactions"</span>;
1349: <span class="kw">import</span> { <span class="prop">suiClient</span>, <span class="prop">CONTRACT</span> } <span class="kw">from</span> <span class="str">"./sui-client"</span>;
1350: <span class="kw">import</span> <span class="kw">type</span> { <span class="ty">SignAndExecuteTransaction</span> } <span class="kw">from</span> <span class="str">"@mysten/dapp-kit"</span>;
1351: 
1352: <span class="cm">/**
1353:  * Issue credential on-chain
1354:  * Dipanggil setelah Walrus upload selesai
1355:  */</span>
1356: <span class="kw">export async function</span> <span class="fn">issueCredentialTx</span>(
1357:   <span class="prop">params</span>: {
1358:     <span class="prop">issuerCapId</span>: <span class="ty">string</span>;
1359:     <span class="prop">walrusBlobId</span>: <span class="ty">string</span>;
1360:     <span class="prop">walrusMetadataBlobId</span>: <span class="ty">string</span>;
1361:     <span class="prop">documentHash</span>: <span class="ty">Uint8Array</span>;
1362:     <span class="prop">credentialType</span>: <span class="ty">string</span>;
1363:     <span class="prop">title</span>: <span class="ty">string</span>;
1364:     <span class="prop">recipient</span>: <span class="ty">string</span>;
1365:     <span class="prop">recipientName</span>: <span class="ty">string</span>;
1366:     <span class="prop">expiresAt</span>: <span class="ty">number</span>; <span class="cm">// 0 = no expiry</span>
1367:   },
1368:   <span class="prop">signAndExecute</span>: <span class="ty">SignAndExecuteTransaction</span>
1369: ) {
1370:   <span class="kw">const</span> <span class="prop">tx</span> = <span class="kw">new</span> <span class="fn">Transaction</span>();
1371: 
1372:   <span class="prop">tx</span>.<span class="fn">moveCall</span>({
1373:     <span class="prop">target</span>: <span class="str">`</span><span class="prop">${CONTRACT.packageId}</span><span class="str">::</span><span class="prop">${CONTRACT.credentialModule}</span><span class="str">::issue_credential`</span>,
1374:     <span class="prop">arguments</span>: [
1375:       <span class="prop">tx</span>.<span class="fn">object</span>(<span class="prop">params</span>.<span class="prop">issuerCapId</span>),
1376:       <span class="prop">tx</span>.<span class="fn">pure</span>.<span class="fn">vector</span>(<span class="str">"u8"</span>, <span class="kw">new</span> <span class="fn">TextEncoder</span>().<span class="fn">encode</span>(<span class="prop">params</span>.<span class="prop">walrusBlobId</span>)),
1377:       <span class="prop">tx</span>.<span class="fn">pure</span>.<span class="fn">vector</span>(<span class="str">"u8"</span>, <span class="kw">new</span> <span class="fn">TextEncoder</span>().<span class="fn">encode</span>(<span class="prop">params</span>.<span class="prop">walrusMetadataBlobId</span>)),
1378:       <span class="prop">tx</span>.<span class="fn">pure</span>.<span class="fn">vector</span>(<span class="str">"u8"</span>, <span class="prop">params</span>.<span class="prop">documentHash</span>),
1379:       <span class="prop">tx</span>.<span class="fn">pure</span>.<span class="fn">vector</span>(<span class="str">"u8"</span>, <span class="kw">new</span> <span class="fn">TextEncoder</span>().<span class="fn">encode</span>(<span class="prop">params</span>.<span class="prop">credentialType</span>)),
1380:       <span class="prop">tx</span>.<span class="fn">pure</span>.<span class="fn">vector</span>(<span class="str">"u8"</span>, <span class="kw">new</span> <span class="fn">TextEncoder</span>().<span class="fn">encode</span>(<span class="prop">params</span>.<span class="prop">title</span>)),
1381:       <span class="prop">tx</span>.<span class="fn">pure</span>.<span class="fn">address</span>(<span class="prop">params</span>.<span class="prop">recipient</span>),
1382:       <span class="prop">tx</span>.<span class="fn">pure</span>.<span class="fn">vector</span>(<span class="str">"u8"</span>, <span class="kw">new</span> <span class="fn">TextEncoder</span>().<span class="fn">encode</span>(<span class="prop">params</span>.<span class="prop">recipientName</span>)),
1383:       <span class="prop">tx</span>.<span class="fn">pure</span>.<span class="fn">u64</span>(<span class="prop">params</span>.<span class="prop">expiresAt</span>),
1384:       <span class="prop">tx</span>.<span class="fn">object</span>(<span class="str">"0x6"</span>), <span class="cm">// Sui Clock object (always 0x6)</span>
1385:     ],
1386:   });
1387: 
1388:   <span class="kw">return</span> <span class="fn">signAndExecute</span>({ <span class="prop">transaction</span>: <span class="prop">tx</span> });
1389: }
1390: 
1391: <span class="cm">/**
1392:  * Query credential object dari SUI via Tatum RPC
1393:  */</span>
1394: <span class="kw">export async function</span> <span class="fn">getCredential</span>(<span class="prop">credentialObjectId</span>: <span class="ty">string</span>) {
1395:   <span class="kw">return</span> <span class="prop">suiClient</span>.<span class="fn">getObject</span>({
1396:     <span class="prop">id</span>: <span class="prop">credentialObjectId</span>,
1397:     <span class="prop">options</span>: {
1398:       <span class="prop">showContent</span>: <span class="kw">true</span>,
1399:       <span class="prop">showOwner</span>: <span class="kw">true</span>,
1400:       <span class="prop">showType</span>: <span class="kw">true</span>,
1401:     },
1402:   });
1403: }
1404: 
1405: <span class="cm">/**
1406:  * Get semua credential milik wallet address tertentu
1407:  */</span>
1408: <span class="kw">export async function</span> <span class="fn">getWalletCredentials</span>(<span class="prop">walletAddress</span>: <span class="ty">string</span>) {
1409:   <span class="kw">const</span> <span class="prop">objects</span> = <span class="kw">await</span> <span class="prop">suiClient</span>.<span class="fn">getOwnedObjects</span>({
1410:     <span class="prop">owner</span>: <span class="prop">walletAddress</span>,
1411:     <span class="prop">filter</span>: {
1412:       <span class="prop">StructType</span>: <span class="str">`</span><span class="prop">${CONTRACT.packageId}</span><span class="str">::credential::Credential`</span>,
1413:     },
1414:     <span class="prop">options</span>: { <span class="prop">showContent</span>: <span class="kw">true</span>, <span class="prop">showType</span>: <span class="kw">true</span> },
1415:   });
1416:   <span class="kw">return</span> <span class="prop">objects</span>.<span class="prop">data</span>;
1417: }
1418:       </div>
1419:     </div>
1420:   </div>
1421: </section>

1424: <section class="section" id="frontend">
1425:   <div class="container">
1426:     <div class="section-label" data-num="07">FRONTEND PAGES</div>
1427:     <h2 class="section-title">Frontend ŌĆö 3 Core Pages</h2>
1428:     <p class="section-desc">Tiga halaman utama yang harus dibangun. Prioritaskan Verifier Page karena ini yang paling sering di-demo ke juri.</p>
1429: 
1430:     <div class="grid-3" style="margin-bottom: 2rem;">
1431:       <div class="card card-green">
1432:         <div class="arch-label" style="text-align:left; color: var(--green); font-size: 10px; margin-bottom: 6px;">PRIORITY 1</div>
1433:         <div style="font-weight: 600; font-size: 15px; margin-bottom: 6px;">Verifier Page</div>
1434:         <p style="font-size: 13px;">Input credential ID / wallet address ŌåÆ instant verification result + preview dokumen dari Walrus. Zero login needed.</p>
1435:         <code style="font-size: 11px;">/verify/[credentialId]</code>
1436:       </div>
1437:       <div class="card card-blue">
1438:         <div class="arch-label" style="text-align:left; color: var(--blue); font-size: 10px; margin-bottom: 6px;">PRIORITY 2</div>
1439:         <div style="font-weight: 600; font-size: 15px; margin-bottom: 6px;">Issuer Dashboard</div>
1440:         <p style="font-size: 13px;">Connect wallet ŌåÆ upload dokumen ke Walrus ŌåÆ fill form ŌåÆ issue credential on-chain via Tatum RPC.</p>
1441:         <code style="font-size: 11px;">/issue</code>
1442:       </div>
1443:       <div class="card">
1444:         <div class="arch-label" style="text-align:left; color: var(--amber); font-size: 10px; margin-bottom: 6px;">PRIORITY 3</div>
1445:         <div style="font-weight: 600; font-size: 15px; margin-bottom: 6px;">Holder Wallet</div>
1446:         <p style="font-size: 13px;">Connect wallet ŌåÆ lihat semua credential ŌåÆ copy share link ŌåÆ share ke employer.</p>
1447:         <code style="font-size: 11px;">/wallet</code>
1448:       </div>
1449:     </div>
1450: 
1451:     <div class="code-wrap">
1452:       <div class="code-header">
1453:         <span class="code-file">app/app/verify/[id]/page.tsx</span>
1454:         <span class="code-desc">Verifier page ŌĆö paling penting untuk demo</span>
1455:       </div>
1456:       <div class="code-block">
1457: <span class="str">"use client"</span>;
1458: <span class="kw">import</span> { <span class="ty">useEffect</span>, <span class="ty">useState</span> } <span class="kw">from</span> <span class="str">"react"</span>;
1459: <span class="kw">import</span> { <span class="fn">getCredential</span> } <span class="kw">from</span> <span class="str">"@/lib/contract"</span>;
1460: <span class="kw">import</span> { <span class="fn">fetchMetadataFromWalrus</span>, <span class="fn">fetchFromWalrus</span> } <span class="kw">from</span> <span class="str">"@/lib/walrus"</span>;
1461: 
1462: <span class="kw">type</span> <span class="ty">VerifyStatus</span> = <span class="str">"loading"</span> | <span class="str">"valid"</span> | <span class="str">"revoked"</span> | <span class="str">"expired"</span> | <span class="str">"not_found"</span>;
1463: 
1464: <span class="kw">export default function</span> <span class="fn">VerifyPage</span>({ <span class="prop">params</span> }: { <span class="prop">params</span>: { <span class="prop">id</span>: <span class="ty">string</span> } }) {
1465:   <span class="kw">const</span> [<span class="prop">status</span>, <span class="fn">setStatus</span>] = <span class="fn">useState</span>&lt;<span class="ty">VerifyStatus</span>&gt;(<span class="str">"loading"</span>);
1466:   <span class="kw">const</span> [<span class="prop">credential</span>, <span class="fn">setCredential</span>] = <span class="fn">useState</span>&lt;<span class="kw">any</span>&gt;(<span class="kw">null</span>);
1467:   <span class="kw">const</span> [<span class="prop">metadata</span>, <span class="fn">setMetadata</span>] = <span class="fn">useState</span>&lt;<span class="kw">any</span>&gt;(<span class="kw">null</span>);
1468:   <span class="kw">const</span> [<span class="prop">docUrl</span>, <span class="fn">setDocUrl</span>] = <span class="fn">useState</span>&lt;<span class="ty">string</span> | <span class="kw">null</span>&gt;(<span class="kw">null</span>);
1469: 
1470:   <span class="fn">useEffect</span>(<span class="kw">async</span> () => {
1471:     <span class="kw">try</span> {
1472:       <span class="cm">// 1. Query credential on-chain via Tatum RPC</span>
1473:       <span class="kw">const</span> <span class="prop">obj</span> = <span class="kw">await</span> <span class="fn">getCredential</span>(<span class="prop">params</span>.<span class="prop">id</span>);
1474:       <span class="kw">if</span> (!<span class="prop">obj</span>.<span class="prop">data</span>) { <span class="fn">setStatus</span>(<span class="str">"not_found"</span>); <span class="kw">return</span>; }
1475: 
1476:       <span class="kw">const</span> <span class="prop">fields</span> = (<span class="prop">obj</span>.<span class="prop">data</span>.<span class="prop">content</span> <span class="kw">as</span> <span class="kw">any</span>).<span class="prop">fields</span>;
1477:       <span class="fn">setCredential</span>(<span class="prop">fields</span>);
1478: 
1479:       <span class="cm">// 2. Check validity</span>
1480:       <span class="kw">if</span> (!<span class="prop">fields</span>.<span class="prop">is_valid</span>) { <span class="fn">setStatus</span>(<span class="str">"revoked"</span>); <span class="kw">return</span>; }
1481:       <span class="kw">const</span> <span class="prop">now</span> = <span class="fn">Date</span>.<span class="fn">now</span>();
1482:       <span class="kw">if</span> (<span class="prop">fields</span>.<span class="prop">expires_at</span> > <span class="num">0</span> && <span class="prop">now</span> > <span class="fn">Number</span>(<span class="prop">fields</span>.<span class="prop">expires_at</span>)) {
1483:         <span class="fn">setStatus</span>(<span class="str">"expired"</span>); <span class="kw">return</span>;
1484:       }
1485: 
1486:       <span class="cm">// 3. Fetch metadata dari Walrus</span>
1487:       <span class="kw">const</span> <span class="prop">meta</span> = <span class="kw">await</span> <span class="fn">fetchMetadataFromWalrus</span>(<span class="prop">fields</span>.<span class="prop">walrus_metadata_blob_id</span>);
1488:       <span class="fn">setMetadata</span>(<span class="prop">meta</span>);
1489: 
1490:       <span class="cm">// 4. Fetch dokumen asli dari Walrus (PDF/image)</span>
1491:       <span class="kw">const</span> <span class="prop">docBlob</span> = <span class="kw">await</span> <span class="fn">fetchFromWalrus</span>(<span class="prop">fields</span>.<span class="prop">walrus_blob_id</span>);
1492:       <span class="fn">setDocUrl</span>(<span class="fn">URL</span>.<span class="fn">createObjectURL</span>(<span class="prop">docBlob</span>));
1493:       <span class="fn">setStatus</span>(<span class="str">"valid"</span>);
1494:     } <span class="kw">catch</span> {
1495:       <span class="fn">setStatus</span>(<span class="str">"not_found"</span>);
1496:     }
1497:   }, [<span class="prop">params</span>.<span class="prop">id</span>]);
1498: 
1499:   <span class="kw">return</span> (
1500:     &lt;<span class="fn">div</span> <span class="prop">className</span>=<span class="str">"max-w-2xl mx-auto p-6"</span>&gt;
1501:       {<span class="prop">status</span> === <span class="str">"loading"</span> && &lt;<span class="fn">VerifyLoading</span> /&gt;}
1502:       {<span class="prop">status</span> === <span class="str">"valid"</span> && &lt;<span class="fn">VerifySuccess</span> <span class="prop">credential</span>={<span class="prop">credential</span>} <span class="prop">metadata</span>={<span class="prop">metadata</span>} <span class="prop">docUrl</span>={<span class="prop">docUrl</span>} /&gt;}
1503:       {<span class="prop">status</span> === <span class="str">"revoked"</span> && &lt;<span class="fn">VerifyRevoked</span> <span class="prop">credential</span>={<span class="prop">credential</span>} /&gt;}
1504:       {<span class="prop">status</span> === <span class="str">"expired"</span> && &lt;<span class="fn">VerifyExpired</span> <span class="prop">credential</span>={<span class="prop">credential</span>} /&gt;}
1505:       {<span class="prop">status</span> === <span class="str">"not_found"</span> && &lt;<span class="fn">VerifyNotFound</span> /&gt;}
1506:     &lt;/<span class="fn">div</span>&gt;
1507:   );
1508: }
1509:       </div>
1510:     </div>
1511: 
1512:     <div class="code-wrap">
1513:       <div class="code-header">
1514:         <span class="code-file">app/.env.local</span>
1515:         <span class="code-desc">Environment variables yang diperlukan</span>
1516:       </div>
1517:       <div class="code-block">
1518: <span class="cm"># Tatum API Key ŌĆö dari dashboard.tatum.io</span>
1519: <span class="prop">TATUM_API_KEY</span>=<span class="str">your_tatum_api_key_here</span>
1520: 
1521: <span class="cm"># SUI Smart Contract (setelah deploy)</span>
1522: <span class="prop">NEXT_PUBLIC_PACKAGE_ID</span>=<span class="str">0x...</span>
1523: <span class="prop">NEXT_PUBLIC_NETWORK</span>=<span class="str">mainnet</span>
1524: 
1525: <span class="cm"># Walrus (tidak perlu API key untuk public endpoints)</span>
1526: <span class="prop">NEXT_PUBLIC_WALRUS_PUBLISHER</span>=<span class="str">https://publisher.walrus-mainnet.walrus.space</span>
1527: <span class="prop">NEXT_PUBLIC_WALRUS_AGGREGATOR</span>=<span class="str">https://aggregator.walrus-mainnet.walrus.space</span>

1533: <!-- ==================== SECTION 8: BACKEND API ==================== -->
1534: <section class="section" id="api">
1535:   <div class="container">
1536:     <div class="section-label" data-num="08">BACKEND API ROUTES</div>
1537:     <h2 class="section-title">API Routes (Next.js)</h2>
1538:     <p class="section-desc">Tiga API route yang menjadi backbone WalTrust. Upload endpoint khususnya kritis karena ini yang handle Walrus integration.</p>
1539: 
1540:     <div class="code-wrap">
1541:       <div class="code-header">
1542:         <span class="code-file">app/app/api/upload/route.ts</span>
1543:         <span class="code-desc">Upload dokumen ke Walrus ŌĆö server-side untuk keamanan</span>
1544:       </div>
1545:       <div class="code-block">
1546: <span class="cm">// app/app/api/upload/route.ts</span>
1547: <span class="kw">import</span> { <span class="ty">NextRequest</span>, <span class="ty">NextResponse</span> } <span class="kw">from</span> <span class="str">"next/server"</span>;
1548: <span class="kw">import</span> { <span class="fn">uploadToWalrus</span>, <span class="fn">uploadMetadataToWalrus</span>, <span class="fn">hashFile</span> } <span class="kw">from</span> <span class="str">"@/lib/walrus"</span>;
1549: 
1550: <span class="kw">export async function</span> <span class="fn">POST</span>(<span class="prop">req</span>: <span class="ty">NextRequest</span>) {
1551:   <span class="kw">try</span> {
1552:     <span class="kw">const</span> <span class="prop">formData</span> = <span class="kw">await</span> <span class="prop">req</span>.<span class="fn">formData</span>();
1553:     <span class="kw">const</span> <span class="prop">file</span> = <span class="prop">formData</span>.<span class="fn">get</span>(<span class="str">"document"</span>) <span class="kw">as</span> <span class="ty">File</span>;
1554:     <span class="kw">const</span> <span class="prop">metadataStr</span> = <span class="prop">formData</span>.<span class="fn">get</span>(<span class="str">"metadata"</span>) <span class="kw">as</span> <span class="ty">string</span>;
1555: 
1556:     <span class="kw">if</span> (!<span class="prop">file</span>) {
1557:       <span class="kw">return</span> <span class="ty">NextResponse</span>.<span class="fn">json</span>({ <span class="prop">error</span>: <span class="str">"No file"</span> }, { <span class="prop">status</span>: <span class="num">400</span> });
1558:     }
1559: 
1560:     <span class="cm">// Validasi file type</span>
1561:     <span class="kw">const</span> <span class="prop">allowedTypes</span> = [<span class="str">"application/pdf"</span>, <span class="str">"image/jpeg"</span>, <span class="str">"image/png"</span>];
1562:     <span class="kw">if</span> (!<span class="prop">allowedTypes</span>.<span class="fn">includes</span>(<span class="prop">file</span>.<span class="prop">type</span>)) {
1563:       <span class="kw">return</span> <span class="ty">NextResponse</span>.<span class="fn">json</span>({ <span class="prop">error</span>: <span class="str">"Invalid file type"</span> }, { <span class="prop">status</span>: <span class="num">400</span> });
1564:     }
1565: 
1566:     <span class="cm">// Max 10MB</span>
1567:     <span class="kw">if</span> (<span class="prop">file</span>.<span class="prop">size</span> > <span class="num">10</span> * <span class="num">1024</span> * <span class="num">1024</span>) {
1568:       <span class="kw">return</span> <span class="ty">NextResponse</span>.<span class="fn">json</span>({ <span class="prop">error</span>: <span class="str">"File too large (max 10MB)"</span> }, { <span class="prop">status</span>: <span class="num">400</span> });
1569:     }
1570: 
1571:     <span class="kw">const</span> <span class="prop">fileBuffer</span> = <span class="kw">await</span> <span class="prop">file</span>.<span class="fn">arrayBuffer</span>();
1572:     <span class="kw">const</span> <span class="prop">fileBytes</span> = <span class="kw">new</span> <span class="fn">Uint8Array</span>(<span class="prop">fileBuffer</span>);
1573: 
1574:     <span class="cm">// Upload dokumen asli + metadata ke Walrus secara paralel</span>
1575:     <span class="kw">const</span> [<span class="prop">docResult</span>, <span class="prop">metaResult</span>, <span class="prop">hash</span>] = <span class="kw">await</span> <span class="fn">Promise</span>.<span class="fn">all</span>([
1576:       <span class="fn">uploadToWalrus</span>(<span class="prop">fileBytes</span>, <span class="prop">file</span>.<span class="prop">type</span>),
1577:       <span class="fn">uploadMetadataToWalrus</span>(<span class="fn">JSON</span>.<span class="fn">parse</span>(<span class="prop">metadataStr</span>)),
1578:       <span class="fn">hashFile</span>(<span class="prop">fileBuffer</span>),
1579:     ]);
1580: 
1581:     <span class="kw">return</span> <span class="ty">NextResponse</span>.<span class="fn">json</span>({
1582:       <span class="prop">documentBlobId</span>: <span class="prop">docResult</span>.<span class="prop">blobId</span>,
1583:       <span class="prop">metadataBlobId</span>: <span class="prop">metaResult</span>.<span class="prop">blobId</span>,
1584:       <span class="prop">documentHash</span>: <span class="fn">Array</span>.<span class="fn">from</span>(<span class="prop">hash</span>),
1585:       <span class="prop">docEndEpoch</span>: <span class="prop">docResult</span>.<span class="prop">endEpoch</span>,
1586:     });
1587:   } <span class="kw">catch</span> (<span class="prop">err</span>) {
1588:     <span class="prop">console</span>.<span class="fn">error</span>(<span class="str">"Upload error:"</span>, <span class="prop">err</span>);
1589:     <span class="kw">return</span> <span class="ty">NextResponse</span>.<span class="fn">json</span>({ <span class="prop">error</span>: <span class="str">"Upload failed"</span> }, { <span class="prop">status</span>: <span class="num">500</span> });
1590:   }
1591: }
1592:       </div>
1593:     </div>
1594:   </div>
1595: </section>

1751:     <h3>README Template Structure</h3>
1752:     <div class="code-wrap">
1753:       <div class="code-block">
1754: <span class="cm"># WalTrust ŌĆö Decentralized Credential Verification</span>
1755: 
1756: <span class="cm">## ­¤Åå Tatum ├Ś Walrus Hackathon Submission</span>
1757: 
1758: <span class="cm">### What is WalTrust?</span>
1759: WalTrust is a trustless credential verification system built on SUI.
1760: Documents live on Walrus. Attestations live on-chain. Verification takes 3 seconds.
1761: 
1762: <span class="cm">### Architecture</span>
1763: [Diagram goes here ŌĆö use draw.io atau Mermaid]
1764: 
1765: SUI Move Contract ŌåÆ stores: credential metadata, blob IDs, validity status
1766: Walrus Storage   ŌåÆ stores: original PDF/image document + metadata JSON
1767: Tatum RPC        ŌåÆ powers: ALL on-chain queries and transaction execution
1768: Next.js Frontend ŌåÆ provides: issue, verify, and wallet management UI
1769: 
1770: <span class="cm">### Tech Stack</span>
1771: - Smart Contract: Sui Move (SUI Mainnet)
1772: - Storage: Walrus (Mainnet)  ŌåÉ CORE, not add-on
1773: - RPC: Tatum (sui-mainnet.gateway.tatum.io)  ŌåÉ ALL calls
1774: - Frontend: Next.js 14 + TypeScript + @mysten/dapp-kit
1775: - Hosting: Vercel
1776: 
1777: <span class="cm">### Live Demo</span>
1778: ­¤īÉ https://waltrust.vercel.app
1779: ­¤ō” Package ID: 0x[mainnet_package_id]
1780: ­¤öŹ SuiScan: https://suiscan.xyz/mainnet/object/[package_id]
1781: 
1782: <span class="cm">### How to Run</span>
1783: 1. git clone https://github.com/[you]/waltrust
1784: 2. cd app && cp .env.example .env.local
1785: 3. Fill in TATUM_API_KEY from dashboard.tatum.io
1786: 4. npm install && npm run dev
1787: 
1788: <span class="cm">### Walrus Integration Details</span>
1789: Every credential stores TWO Walrus blobs:
1790: - walrus_blob_id: The actual document (PDF/image)
1791: - walrus_metadata_blob_id: JSON metadata for quick display
1792: Both Blob IDs are stored on-chain in the SUI Move object.
1793: Revocation: 1 on-chain tx. No Walrus update needed ŌĆö blob stays, chain says REVOKED.
1794:       </div>
1795:     </div>
1796:
