Now the issue-content and wallet-content:

**Tool: write**

**Input:**
```json
{
  "content": "\"use client\";\n\nimport { useState, useRef } from \"react\";\nimport { useCurrentAccount, useSignAndExecuteTransaction } from \"@mysten/dapp-kit\";\nimport { uploadToWalrus, uploadMetadataToWalrus, hashFile } from \"@/lib/walrus\";\nimport { buildIssueCredentialTx } from \"@/lib/contract\";\nimport { WALTRUST_CONSTANTS } from \"@/lib/utils\";\nimport { ConnectButton } from \"@mysten/dapp-kit\";\nimport { FileUp, Check, Loader2, AlertCircle, Shield, ArrowRight } from \"lucide-react\";\nimport { useGsapReveal, useMagneticHover } from \"@/lib/gsap-hooks\";\n\ntype IssueStep = \"form\" | \"uploading\" | \"signing\" | \"success\" | \"error\";\n\nexport function IssueContent() {\n  const account = useCurrentAccount();\n  const { mutateAsync: signAndExecute } = useSignAndExecuteTransaction();\n  const sectionRef = useRef<HTMLElement>(null);\n  const formRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null);\n  const submitRef = useRef<HTMLButtonElement>(null);\n\n  useGsapReveal(sectionRef, { animation: \"up\" });\n  useMagneticHover(submitRef, { strength: 0.15 });\n\n  const [step, setStep] = useState<IssueStep>(\"form\");\n  const [error, setError] = useState(\"\");\n  const [result, setResult] = useState<{ credentialId: string; digest: string } | null>(null);\n\n  const [form, setForm] = useState({\n    issuerCapId: \"\",\n    credentialType: \"degree\",\n    title: \"\",\n    recipient: \"\",\n    recipientName: \"\",\n    expiresAt: \"\",\n  });\n  const [file, setFile] = useState<File | null>(null);\n\n  const handleIssue = async () => {\n    if (!account || !file) return;\n    try {\n      setStep(\"uploading\");\n      setError(\"\");\n      const fileBuffer = await file.arrayBuffer();\n      const fileBytes = new Uint8Array(fileBuffer);\n      const metadata = {\n        title: form.title,\n        credentialType: form.credentialType,\n        issuerName: \"WalTrust Demo Issuer\",\n        recipientName: form.recipientName,\n        issuedAt: new Date().toISOString(),\n        expiresAt: form.expiresAt || null,\n        additionalInfo: {},\n      };\n      const [docResult, metaResult, hash] = await Promise.all([\n        uploadToWalrus(fileBytes, file.type),\n        uploadMetadataToWalrus(metadata),\n        hashFile(fileBuffer),\n      ]);\n      setStep(\"signing\");\n      const tx = buildIssueCredentialTx({\n        issuerCapId: form.issuerCapId,\n        walrusBlobId: docResult.blobId,\n        walrusMetadataBlobId: metaResult.blobId,\n        documentHash: Array.from(hash),\n        credentialType: form.credentialType,\n        title: form.title,\n        recipient: form.recipient,\n        recipientName: form.recipientName,\n        expiresAt: form.expiresAt ? new Date(form.expiresAt).getTime() : 0,\n      });\n      const execResult = await signAndExecute({ transaction: tx });\n      setResult({ credentialId: execResult.digest, digest: execResult.digest });\n      setStep(\"success\");\n    } catch (err: any) {\n      setError(err?.message || \"Transaction failed\");\n      setStep(\"error\");\n    }\n  };\n\n  if (!account) {\n    return (\n      <div className=\"max-w-2xl mx-auto px-4 py-20 text-center\">\n        <div className=\"neo-card shadow-neo-pink inline-block p-12\">\n          <Shield className=\"w-16 h-16 text-neo-pink mx-auto mb-4\" strokeWidth={3} />\n          <h1 className=\"font-display font-800 text-3xl mb-3 uppercase\">Issuer Dashboard</h1>\n          <p className=\"font-mono text-sm text-neo-text2 mb-6\">Connect wallet to issue credentials</p>\n          <div className=\"[&_button]:!bg-neo-green [&_button]:!border-[3px] [&_button]:!border-neo-border\n            [&_button]:!rounded-neo [&_button]:!shadow-neo [&_button]:!font-mono [&_button]:!text-sm\n            [&_button]:!font-bold [&_button]:!uppercase [&_button]:!tracking-wider\">\n            <ConnectButton />\n          </div>\n        </div>\n      </div>\n    );\n  }\n\n  return (\n    <section ref={sectionRef} className=\"max-w-2xl mx-auto px-4 sm:px-6 py-10\">\n      <div className=\"neo-section-label\">02 // Issuer</div>\n      <h1 {
```
```json
  "content": "\"use client\";\n\nimport { useEffect, useState, useRef } from \"react\";\nimport { getCredential, parseCredentialFields, CredentialFields, checkCredentialValidity } from \"@/lib/contract\";\nimport { VerifyResult } from \"@/components/verify-result\";\nimport { useGsapReveal } from \"@/lib/gsap-hooks\";\n\ntype VerifyStatus = \"loading\" | \"valid\" | \"revoked\" | \"expired\" | \"not_found\";\n\nexport function VerifyContent({ id }: { id: string }) {\n  const [status, setStatus] = useState<VerifyStatus>(\"loading\");\n  const [credential, setCredential] = useState<CredentialFields | null>(null);\n  const sectionRef = useRef<HTMLElement>(null);\n\n  useGsapReveal(sectionRef, { animation: \"up\" });\n\n  useEffect(() => {\n    if (!id) { setStatus(\"not_found\"); return; }\n    getCredential(id)\n      .then((obj) => {\n        const fields = parseCredentialFields(obj);\n        if (!fields) { setStatus(\"not_found\"); return; }\n        setCredential(fields);\n        setStatus(checkCredentialValidity(fields));\n      })\n      .catch(() => setStatus(\"not_found\"));\n  }, [id]);\n\n  return (\n    <section ref={sectionRef} className=\"max-w-2xl mx-auto px-4 sm:px-6 py-10\">\n      <div className=\"neo-section-label\">01 // Verify</div>\n      <h1 className=\"font-display font-800 text-3xl sm:text-4xl tracking-tight uppercase mb-2\">\n        Verify <span className=\"text-neo-green\">Credential</span>\n      </h1>\n      <p className=\"font-mono text-xs text-neo-text3 mb-8 uppercase tracking-wider\">\n        ID: {id?.slice(0, 12)}...{id?.slice(-8)}\n      </p>\n      <VerifyResult status={status} credential={credential} objectId={id} />\n    </section>\n  );\n}\n",
  "filePath": "/Users/macbookair/Documents/project/WalTrust/app/components/verify-content.tsx"
}
```
